// ============================================================
// UTILITY COMPONENTS

const Badge = ({ color, children, size = "sm" }) => {
  const colors = {
    green: "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400 border-green-500/30",
    red: "bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border-red-500/30",
    amber: "bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-400 border-amber-500/30",
    blue: "bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400 border-blue-500/30",
    purple: "bg-purple-500/20 text-purple-400 border-purple-500/30",
    slate: "bg-slate-500/20 text-gray-900 border-slate-500/30",
  };
  return (
    <span className={`inline-flex items-center border rounded-full font-medium ${size === "xs" ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-xs" : "px-3 py-1 text-sm"} ${colors[color] || colors.blue}`}>
      {children}
    </span>
  );
};

const StatCard = ({ label, value, sub, icon, color = "orange" }) => {
  const colorMap = {
    orange: "from-orange-500/20 to-orange-600/10 border-orange-500/20",
    green: "from-green-500/20 to-green-600/10 border-green-500/20",
    blue: "from-blue-500/20 to-blue-600/10 border-blue-500/20",
    purple: "from-purple-500/20 to-purple-600/10 border-purple-500/20",
  };
  const iconColorMap = {
    orange: "text-orange-400",
    green: "text-green-400",
    blue: "text-blue-400",
    purple: "text-purple-400",
  };
  return (
    <div className={`bg-gradient-to-br ${colorMap[color]} border rounded-2xl p-5`}>
      <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
        <div>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold mb-1">{label}</p>
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-1">{value}</p>
          {sub && <p className="text-gray-800 text-xs">{sub}</p>}
        </div>
        <span className={`text-3xl ${iconColorMap[color]}`}>{icon}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

const Modal = ({ open, onClose, title, children, size = "md" }) => {
  // Prevent body scroll when modal open
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (open) { document.body.style.overflow = "hidden"; }
    return () => { document.body.style.overflow = ""; };
  }, [open]);

  if (!open) return null;
  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex flex-col justify-end sm:justify-center sm:items-center sm:p-4"
      style={{touchAction:"none"}}>
      <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-black/60 backdrop-blur-sm" onClick={onClose} />
      {/* Bottom sheet — rises above keyboard automatically */}
      <div className="relative w-full sm:max-w-lg bg-white rounded-t-3xl sm:rounded-2xl shadow-2xl z-10 flex flex-col"
        style={{ maxHeight:"85dvh", maxWidth:"512px" }}>
        {/* Drag handle */}
        <div className="flex justify-center pt-3 pb-1 shrink-0">
          <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-300 rounded-full" />
        </div>
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-b border-gray-100 shrink-0">
          <h3 className="text-base font-extrabold text-gray-900">{title}</h3>
          <button onClick={onClose}
            className="w-10 h-10 flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-gray-100 active:bg-red-100 text-gray-500 font-bold text-lg transition">✕</button>
        </div>
        {/* Scrollable body */}
        <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-5 py-4 pb-8" style={{WebkitOverflowScrolling:"touch"}}>{children}</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// Mobile-friendly Input — 16px font prevents iOS zoom
const Input = ({ label, labelHindi, className = "", type, ...props }) => (
  <div className="space-y-1.5">
    {label && (
      <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">
        {label}{labelHindi && <span className="text-gray-500 font-normal ml-1">({labelHindi})</span>}
      </label>
    )}
    <input
      type={type}
      inputMode={type === "number" ? "numeric" : type === "tel" ? "tel" : undefined}
      pattern={type === "number" ? "[0-9]*" : undefined}
      {...props}
      className={`w-full bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3.5 text-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 focus:bg-white placeholder-gray-400 transition ${className}`}
      style={{ fontSize: "16px" }}
    />
  </div>
);

// Mobile-friendly Select — 16px font prevents iOS zoom
const Select = ({ label, labelHindi, children, ...props }) => (
  <div className="space-y-1.5">
    {label && (
      <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-800">
        {label}{labelHindi && <span className="text-gray-500 font-normal ml-1">({labelHindi})</span>}
      </label>
    )}
    <div className="relative">
      <select
        {...props}
        className="w-full bg-gray-50 border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3.5 text-gray-900 focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400 focus:bg-white transition appearance-none pr-10"
        style={{ fontSize: "16px" }}
      >
        {children}
      </select>
      <span className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none">▾</span>
    </div>
  </div>
);

const Btn = ({ children, variant = "primary", size = "md", className = "", disabled = false, ...props }) => {
  const variants = {
    primary:   "bg-orange-500 active:bg-orange-600 text-white shadow-sm shadow-orange-200",
    secondary: "bg-gray-100 active:bg-gray-200 text-gray-800 border border-gray-200",
    danger:    "bg-red-50 active:bg-red-100 text-red-600 border border-red-200",
    success:   "bg-green-50 active:bg-green-100 text-green-700 border border-green-200",
    ghost:     "active:bg-gray-100 text-gray-700",
  };
  // minimum 44px touch target
  const sizes = { sm: "px-4 py-2.5 text-sm min-h-[40px]", md: "px-5 py-3.5 text-sm min-h-[48px]", lg: "px-6 py-4 text-base min-h-[52px]" };
  return (
    <button
      {...props}
      disabled={disabled}
      className={`${variants[variant]} ${sizes[size]} rounded-2xl font-semibold transition-all active:scale-95 ${disabled ? "opacity-40 cursor-not-allowed pointer-events-none" : ""} ${className}`}
    >
      {children}
    </button>
  );
};

const Table = ({ headers, rows, emptyMsg = "कोई data नहीं" }) => (
  <div className="overflow-x-auto rounded-2xl border border-gray-200">
    <table className="w-full text-sm">
      <thead>
        <tr className="bg-gray-800">
          {headers.map((h, i) => (
            <th key={i} className="px-4 py-3 text-left text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide whitespace-nowrap">{h}</th>
          ))}
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody className="divide-y divide-gray-100">
        {rows.length === 0
          ? <tr><td colSpan={headers.length} className="text-center py-12 text-gray-400">{emptyMsg}</td></tr>
          : rows.map((row, i) => <tr key={i} className={i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/50"}>{row}</tr>)
        }
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
);

const Td = ({ children, className = "" }) => (
  <td className={`px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 whitespace-nowrap ${className}`}>{children}</td>
);

// ── Pagination Utility ──────────────────────────────────────
const usePagination = (data, pageSize = 25) => {
  const [page, setPage] = useState(1);
  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(data.length / pageSize));
  const paged = data.slice((page - 1) * pageSize, page * pageSize);
  useEffect(() => { setPage(1); }, [data.length]);
  return { paged, page, setPage, totalPages, total: data.length, pageSize };
};

const Paginator = ({ page, setPage, totalPages, total, pageSize }) => {
  if (totalPages <= 1) return null;
  const from = (page - 1) * pageSize + 1;
  const to   = Math.min(page * pageSize, total);
  const pages = Array.from({ length: Math.min(5, totalPages) }, (_, i) => {
    if (totalPages <= 5) return i + 1;
    if (page <= 3) return i + 1;
    if (page >= totalPages - 2) return totalPages - 4 + i;
    return page - 2 + i;
  });
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2.5 bg-gray-50 border-t border-gray-100">
      <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">{from}–{to} of {total}</span>
      <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
        <button onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.max(1, p - 1))} disabled={page === 1}
          className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 disabled:opacity-30 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300 transition">&lt;</button>
        {pages.map(p => (
          <button key={p} onClick={() => setPage(p)}
            className={"w-7 h-7 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition " +
              (p === page ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "border-gray-200 text-gray-600 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300")}>
            {p}
          </button>
        ))}
        <button onClick={() => setPage(p => Math.min(totalPages, p + 1))} disabled={page === totalPages}
          className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 disabled:opacity-30 hover:bg-orange-50 hover:border-orange-300 transition">&gt;</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// LOGIN
const LoginPage = ({ onLogin }) => {
  const [screen,   setScreen]   = useState("login"); // "login" | "register" | "success"
  const [mobile,   setMobile]   = useState("9876543210");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("admin123");
  const [role,     setRole]     = useState("admin");
  const [loading,  setLoading]  = useState(false);
  const [err,      setErr]      = useState("");

  // Registration form state
  const [reg, setReg] = useState({
    name: "", mobile: "", password: "", confirm: "",
    department: "", aadhaar: "", address: "", emergency: "",
  });
  const [regErr,  setRegErr]  = useState("");
  const [regStep, setRegStep] = useState(1); // 1 = personal, 2 = work

  const handleLogin = () => {
    setLoading(true); setErr("");
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (mobile && password) { onLogin({ ...MOCK_DB.currentUser, role }); }
      else { setErr("Invalid credentials"); }
      setLoading(false);
    }, 800);
  };

  const handleRegNext = () => {
    if (!reg.name.trim())                          { setRegErr("नाम जरूरी है।"); return; }
    if (!/^\d{10}$/.test(reg.mobile))             { setRegErr("10 अंकों का मोबाइल नंबर डालें।"); return; }
    if (reg.password.length < 6)                  { setRegErr("Password कम से कम 6 characters का होना चाहिए।"); return; }
    if (reg.password !== reg.confirm)             { setRegErr("Password और Confirm Password मेल नहीं खाते।"); return; }
    setRegErr(""); setRegStep(2);
  };

  const handleRegSubmit = () => {
    if (!reg.department)                          { setRegErr("Department चुनें।"); return; }
    setLoading(true); setRegErr("");
    setTimeout(() => { setLoading(false); setScreen("success"); }, 1000);
  };

  const setField = (key) => (e) => setReg(p => ({ ...p, [key]: e.target.value }));

  /* ── SUCCESS SCREEN ── */
  if (screen === "success") return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-white flex items-center justify-center p-4"
      style={{ backgroundImage: "radial-gradient(ellipse at 20% 50%, rgba(249,115,22,0.08) 0%, transparent 60%)" }}>
      <div className="w-full max-w-md text-center">
        <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-green-100 rounded-3xl flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-5">
          <svg width="36" height="36" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
            <path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16A34A" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
          </svg>
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-extrabold text-gray-900 mb-2">Registration Submitted!</h2>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mb-1">आपकी request भेज दी गई है।</p>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mb-6">Admin approval के बाद आप login कर पाएंगे।</p>
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl p-4 mb-6 text-left space-y-2">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Name</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.name}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Mobile</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.mobile}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Department</span><span className="font-bold text-gray-900">{reg.department}</span></div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-sm"><span className="text-gray-500">Status</span><span className="font-bold text-amber-600">Pending Approval</span></div>
        </div>
        <button onClick={() => { setScreen("login"); setReg({ name:"",mobile:"",password:"",confirm:"",department:"",aadhaar:"",address:"",emergency:"" }); setRegStep(1); }}
          className="w-full bg-orange-500 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition shadow-md shadow-orange-200">
          Back to Login

  /* ── REGISTER SCREEN ── */
  if (screen === "register") return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-white flex items-center justify-center p-4"
      style={{ backgroundImage: "radial-gradient(ellipse at 80% 20%, rgba(59,130,246,0.06) 0%, transparent 50%)" }}>

        {/* Back to Login */}

          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm mb-5 active:opacity-70 transition">
          <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
            <path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
          </svg>
          Login पर वापस जाएं
        </button>

          <div className="inline-flex items-center justify-center w-14 h-14 mb-3">

        </div>

        {/* Step indicator */}

      style:style?.styleName||"", operation:op?.name||"",

  };

        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Approved list */}
      <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Approved Entries</p>
      {approved.length === 0 && (

          <p className="text-gray-400">कोई approved entry नहीं</p>
        </div>
      )}
      <div className="space-y-2">
        {approved.map(e=>(
          <div key={e.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-3.5">
            <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-green-50 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">

            </div>

              <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{e.style}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.operation} · {e.date}</p>
