const STATUS_COLORS = { Draft: "slate", Active: "blue", Completed: "green", Closed: "red" };
const PROCESS_OPTIONS = ["Cutting", "Stitching", "Overlock", "Finishing", "Packing", "QC", "Embroidery", "Ironing"];

const StyleFiles = () => {
  const [files, setFiles]           = useState(INIT_STYLE_FILES);
  const [view, setView]             = useState("list");       // list | detail | new
  const [selected, setSelected]     = useState(null);
  const [detailTab, setDetailTab]   = useState("info");       // info | processes | entries | payment
  const [search, setSearch]         = useState("");
  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState("all");
  const [showStyleModal, setShowStyleModal] = useState(false);
  const [showProcessModal, setShowProcessModal] = useState(false);
  const [showEntryModal, setShowEntryModal]   = useState(false);
  const [error, setError]           = useState("");
  const [toast, setToast]           = useState("");

  // Style entries per style
  const [allEntries, setAllEntries] = useState([
    { id: "we1", styleId: "sf1", workerName: "Sunita Devi",  staffId: "SG001", process: "Stitching", quantity: 120, date: "2024-01-15", status: "approved", amount: 1800 },
    { id: "we2", styleId: "sf1", workerName: "Ramesh Kumar", staffId: "SG002", process: "Cutting",   quantity: 200, date: "2024-01-15", status: "pending",  amount: 400  },
    { id: "we3", styleId: "sf2", workerName: "Priya Singh",  staffId: "SG003", process: "Finishing", quantity: 80,  date: "2024-01-14", status: "approved", amount: 320  },
    { id: "we4", styleId: "sf3", workerName: "Geeta Rani",   staffId: "SG005", process: "Stitching", quantity: 95,  date: "2024-01-15", status: "pending",  amount: 950  },
  ]);

  const emptyStyleForm = { styleCode: "", styleName: "", buyerName: "", fabricType: "", color: "", sizeRange: "", orderQuantity: "", deliveryDate: "", status: "Draft" };
  const [styleForm, setStyleForm]   = useState(emptyStyleForm);

  const emptyProcess = { name: "Stitching", pieceRate: "" };
  const [processForm, setProcessForm] = useState(emptyProcess);

  const emptyEntry = { workerName: "", staffId: "", process: "", quantity: "", date: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0] };
  const [entryForm, setEntryForm]   = useState(emptyEntry);

  const flash = (msg) => { setToast(msg); setTimeout(() => setToast(""), 2500); };

  // ── Style CRUD ──
  const addStyle = () => {
    if (!styleForm.styleCode || !styleForm.styleName || !styleForm.buyerName || !styleForm.orderQuantity || !styleForm.deliveryDate) {
      setError("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return;
    }
    if (+styleForm.orderQuantity <= 0) { setError("Order quantity 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }
    if (files.find(f => f.styleCode === styleForm.styleCode)) { setError("Style Code already exists!"); return; }
    const newFile = { ...styleForm, id: "sf" + Date.now(), orderQuantity: +styleForm.orderQuantity, processes: [] };
    setFiles([newFile, ...files]);
    setShowStyleModal(false);
    setStyleForm(emptyStyleForm);
    setError("");
    flash("Style File created!");
  };

  const updateStatus = (id, status) => {
    setFiles(files.map(f => f.id === id ? { ...f, status } : f));
    if (selected?.id === id) setSelected(prev => ({ ...prev, status }));
  };

  // ── Process CRUD ──
  const addProcess = () => {
    if (!processForm.name || !processForm.pieceRate || +processForm.pieceRate <= 0) {
      setError("Process name और piece rate भरें।"); return;
    }
    const updated = files.map(f => f.id === selected.id
      ? { ...f, processes: [...f.processes, { id: "p" + Date.now(), name: processForm.name, pieceRate: +processForm.pieceRate }] }
      : f
    );
    setFiles(updated);
    setSelected(updated.find(f => f.id === selected.id));
    setShowProcessModal(false);
    setProcessForm(emptyProcess);
    setError("");
    flash("Process added!");
  };

  const deleteProcess = (pid) => {
    const updated = files.map(f => f.id === selected.id
      ? { ...f, processes: f.processes.filter(p => p.id !== pid) }
      : f
    );
    setFiles(updated);
    setSelected(updated.find(f => f.id === selected.id));
  };

  // ── Work Entry ──
  const addEntry = () => {
    if (!entryForm.workerName || !entryForm.process || !entryForm.quantity || !entryForm.date) {
      setError("सभी fields भरना जरूरी है।"); return;
    }
    if (selected.status === "Closed") { setError("Closed style में entry नहीं हो सकती।"); return; }
    const qty = +entryForm.quantity;
    if (qty <= 0) { setError("Quantity 0 से ज्यादा होनी चाहिए।"); return; }

    // Duplicate check
    const dup = allEntries.find(e =>
      e.styleId === selected.id &&
      e.workerName === entryForm.workerName &&
      e.process === entryForm.process &&
      e.date === entryForm.date &&
      e.status !== "rejected"
    );
    if (dup) { setError("Duplicate entry! Same worker, same process, same date."); return; }

    // Quantity check
    const totalDone = allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === selected.id && e.status === "approved").reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);
    if (totalDone + qty > selected.orderQuantity) {
      setError("Order quantity exceed हो जाएगी! Remaining: " + (selected.orderQuantity - totalDone)); return;
    }

    const proc = selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process);
    const amount = qty * (proc?.pieceRate || 0);
    const newEntry = {
      id: "we" + Date.now(), styleId: selected.id,
      workerName: entryForm.workerName, staffId: entryForm.staffId,
      process: entryForm.process, quantity: qty,
      date: entryForm.date, status: "pending", amount,
    };
    setAllEntries([newEntry, ...allEntries]);
    setShowEntryModal(false);
    setEntryForm(emptyEntry);
    setError("");
    flash("Entry submitted!");
  };

  const approveEntry = (id) => { setAllEntries(allEntries.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status: "approved" } : e)); flash("Approved!"); };
  const rejectEntry  = (id) => { setAllEntries(allEntries.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status: "rejected" } : e)); flash("Rejected."); };

  // ── Derived ──
  const filtered = files
    .filter(f => filterStatus === "all" || f.status === filterStatus)
    .filter(f => !search || f.styleName.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || f.styleCode.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || f.buyerName.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));

  const { paged: pagedStyles, page: sfPage, setPage: setSfPage, totalPages: sfTotalPages, total: sfTotal, pageSize: sfPageSize } = usePagination(filtered, 15);

  const styleEntries = selected ? allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === selected.id) : [];
  const approvedEntries = styleEntries.filter(e => e.status === "approved");
  const totalProduced = approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);

  // Payment summary per worker
  const paymentByWorker = approvedEntries.reduce((acc, e) => {
    if (!acc[e.workerName]) acc[e.workerName] = { workerName: e.workerName, staffId: e.staffId, pieces: 0, amount: 0 };
    acc[e.workerName].pieces += e.quantity;
    acc[e.workerName].amount += e.amount;
    return acc;
  }, {});

  // ── DETAIL VIEW ──
  if (view === "detail" && selected) {
    const progress = selected.orderQuantity > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((totalProduced / selected.orderQuantity) * 100)) : 0;
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}

        {/* Back + title */}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <button onClick={() => { setView("list"); setSelected(null); }} className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 text-orange-600 text-sm font-bold">← Back</button>
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-lg font-extrabold text-gray-900">{selected.styleName}</h1>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{selected.styleCode} • {selected.buyerName}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="ml-auto">
            <Badge color={STATUS_COLORS[selected.status] || "blue"} size="xs">{selected.status}</Badge>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Progress bar */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 px-4 py-3">
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-500 mb-1.5">
            <span>{totalProduced.toLocaleString()} produced</span>
            <span className="font-bold text-orange-500">{progress}%</span>
            <span>{selected.orderQuantity.toLocaleString()} ordered</span>
          </div>
          <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-2.5">
            <div className="h-2.5 rounded-full transition-all" style={{ width: progress + "%", background: progress === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Tabs */}
        <div className="flex gap-2 overflow-x-auto pb-1">
          {[["info","Info"],["processes","Processes"],["entries","Entries"],["payment","Payment"]].map(([k, l]) => (
            <button key={k} onClick={() => setDetailTab(k)}
              className={"px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold whitespace-nowrap border transition " +
                (detailTab === k ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200")}>
              {l}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* TAB: INFO */}
        {detailTab === "info" && (
          <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
            {[
              ["Style Code",      selected.styleCode],
              ["Style Name",      selected.styleName],
              ["Buyer",           selected.buyerName],
              ["Fabric Type",     selected.fabricType],
              ["Color",           selected.color],
              ["Size Range",      selected.sizeRange],
              ["Order Quantity",  selected.orderQuantity.toLocaleString() + " pcs"],
              ["Delivery Date",   selected.deliveryDate],
              ["Status",          selected.status],
            ].map(([label, val]) => (
              <div key={label} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
                <span className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{label}</span>
                <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold">{val}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
            {/* Status change */}
            <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {["Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => (
                <button key={s} onClick={() => updateStatus(selected.id, s)}
                  className={"px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold border transition " +
                    (selected.status === s ? "bg-gray-800 text-white border-gray-800" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200 hover:border-orange-400")}>
                  {s}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: PROCESSES */}
        {detailTab === "processes" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">{selected.processes.length} processes configured</p>
              <Btn size="sm" onClick={() => { setShowProcessModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ Add Process</Btn>
            </div>
            {selected.processes.length === 0 && (
              <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-8 text-center text-gray-400">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-2 rounded-xl bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 15a3 3 0 1 0 0-6 3 3 0 0 0 0 6z" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5"/><path d="M19.4 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 .33 1.82l.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83 2.83l-.06-.06a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82-.33 1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1 1.51V21a2 2 0 0 1-4 0v-.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 19.4a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.82.33l-.06.06a2 2 0 0 1-2.83-2.83l.06-.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.68 15a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51-1H3a2 2 0 0 1 0-4h.09A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 4.6 9a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-.33-1.82l-.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83-2.83l.06.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 9 4.68a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1-1.51V3a2 2 0 0 1 4 0v.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1 1.51 1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.82-.33l.06-.06a2 2 0 0 1 2.83 2.83l-.06.06A1.65 1.65 0 0 0 19.4 9a1.65 1.65 0 0 0 1.51 1H21a2 2 0 0 1 0 4h-.09a1.65 1.65 0 0 0-1.51 1z" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.5"/></svg></div>
                <p className="text-sm font-semibold">No processes yet</p>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              {selected.processes.length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-3 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                  <div>Process</div>
                  <div className="text-center">Piece Rate</div>
                  <div className="text-right">Action</div>
                </div>
              )}
              {selected.processes.map((p, i) => (
                <div key={p.id} className={"grid grid-cols-3 px-4 py-3.5 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <span className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{p.name}</span>
                  <span className="text-center text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {p.pieceRate}/pc</span>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <button onClick={() => deleteProcess(p.id)} className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600 text-xs font-bold">Remove</button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            <Modal open={showProcessModal} onClose={() => { setShowProcessModal(false); setError(""); }} title="Add Process">
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
                <Select label="Process Name" value={processForm.name} onChange={e => setProcessForm({ ...processForm, name: e.target.value })}>
                  {PROCESS_OPTIONS.map(p => <option key={p}>{p}</option>)}
                </Select>
                <Input label="Piece Rate (Rs)" type="number" step="0.5" value={processForm.pieceRate} onChange={e => setProcessForm({ ...processForm, pieceRate: e.target.value })} placeholder="15" />
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowProcessModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
                  <Btn onClick={addProcess} className="flex-1">Add Process</Btn>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Modal>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: ENTRIES */}
        {detailTab === "entries" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">{styleEntries.length} entries</p>
              {selected.status !== "Closed" && (
                <Btn size="sm" onClick={() => { setShowEntryModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ Add Entry</Btn>
              )}
            </div>
            {selected.status === "Closed" && (
              <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold text-center">
                Closed style — no new entries allowed
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Entry list */}
            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              {styleEntries.length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                  <div className="col-span-3">Worker</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2">Process</div>
                  <div className="col-span-1 text-center">Qty</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Amount</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Status</div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">Action</div>
                </div>
              )}
              {styleEntries.length === 0 && <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं</p>}
              {styleEntries.map((e, i) => (
                <div key={e.id} className={"grid grid-cols-12 gap-1 px-4 py-3 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <div className="col-span-3 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs truncate">{e.workerName.split(" ")[0]}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.date}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2">
                    <span className="text-xs bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-semibold">{e.process}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-1 text-center">
                    <span className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{e.quantity}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">
                    <span className="text-green-600 font-bold text-xs">Rs {e.amount}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-center">
                    <Badge color={e.status === "approved" ? "green" : e.status === "rejected" ? "red" : "amber"} size="xs">
                      {e.status}
                    </Badge>
                  </div>
                  <div className="col-span-2 flex gap-1 justify-center">
                    {e.status === "pending" && (
                      <>
                        <button onClick={() => approveEntry(e.id)} className="text-green-600 text-xs font-bold hover:underline">✓</button>
                        <button onClick={() => rejectEntry(e.id)}  className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold hover:underline">✗</button>
                      </>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            <Modal open={showEntryModal} onClose={() => { setShowEntryModal(false); setError(""); }} title="New Work Entry">
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold whitespace-pre-line">{error}</div>}
                <Select label="Worker" value={entryForm.workerName} onChange={e => {
                  const w = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.name === e.target.value);
                  setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, workerName: e.target.value, staffId: w?.staffId || "" });
                }}>
                  <option value="">Select Worker</option>
                  {MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.status === "active").map(w => <option key={w.id} value={w.name}>{w.name} ({w.staffId})</option>)}
                </Select>
                <Select label="Process" value={entryForm.process} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, process: e.target.value })}>
                  <option value="">Select Process</option>
                  {selected.processes.map(p => <option key={p.id} value={p.name}>{p.name} — Rs {p.pieceRate}/pc</option>)}
                </Select>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  <Input label="Quantity" type="number" value={entryForm.quantity} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, quantity: e.target.value })} placeholder="100" />
                  <Input label="Date" type="date" value={entryForm.date} onChange={e => setEntryForm({ ...entryForm, date: e.target.value })} />
                </div>
                {entryForm.process && entryForm.quantity && (
                  <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm">
                    <span className="text-gray-600">Auto Amount: </span>
                    <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-base">
                      Rs {(+entryForm.quantity * (selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process)?.pieceRate || 0)).toLocaleString()}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs ml-1">
                      ({entryForm.quantity} × Rs {selected.processes.find(p => p.name === entryForm.process)?.pieceRate || 0})
                    </span>
                  </div>
                )}
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowEntryModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
                  <Btn onClick={addEntry} className="flex-1">Submit Entry</Btn>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Modal>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* TAB: PAYMENT */}
        {detailTab === "payment" && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex justify-between items-center">
              <span className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-bold">Total Payout (Approved)</span>
              <span className="text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-lg">
                Rs {approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0).toLocaleString()}
              </span>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
                <div className="col-span-2">Worker</div>
                <div className="text-center">Pieces</div>
                <div className="text-right">Amount</div>
              </div>
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).length === 0 && (
                <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm">No approved entries yet</p>
              )}
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).map((w, i) => (
                <div key={w.workerName} className={"grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-3.5 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
                  <div className="col-span-2 flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-xs shrink-0">
                      {w.workerName.charAt(0)}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{w.workerName}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-center">
                    <span className="text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{w.pieces} pcs</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {w.amount.toLocaleString()}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
              {Object.values(paymentByWorker).length > 0 && (
                <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold">
                  <div className="col-span-2 text-gray-300">TOTAL</div>
                  <div className="text-center text-orange-400">{approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0)} pcs</div>
                  <div className="text-right text-green-400">Rs {approvedEntries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0).toLocaleString()}</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* Formula info */}
            <div className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-blue-700">
              <p className="font-bold mb-1">Auto Payment Formula:</p>
              <p>Payment = Quantity × Piece Rate</p>
              <p className="mt-1 text-blue-500">Example: 100 pcs × Rs 15 = Rs 1,500</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ── LIST VIEW ──
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}

      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Style Files</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{files.length} styles — {files.filter(f => f.status === "Active").length} active</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={() => { setShowStyleModal(true); setError(""); }}>+ New Style</Btn>
      </div>

      {/* Search + filter */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
        <input value={search} onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search style, buyer..."
          className="flex-1 min-w-[160px] bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400" />
        <div className="flex gap-1.5 flex-wrap">
          {["all","Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => (
            <button key={s} onClick={() => setFilterStatus(s)}
              className={"px-3 py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold border transition " +
                (filterStatus === s ? "bg-orange-500 text-white border-orange-500" : "bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-200")}>
              {s === "all" ? "All" : s}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Style cards */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {filtered.length === 0 && <p className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200">कोई style नहीं मिली</p>}
        {pagedStyles.map(f => {
          const entries = allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === f.id && e.status === "approved");
          const produced = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.quantity, 0);
          const progress = f.orderQuantity > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((produced / f.orderQuantity) * 100)) : 0;
          const daysLeft = Math.ceil((new Date(f.deliveryDate) - new Date()) / 86400000);
          return (
            <div key={f.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 border-gray-100 hover:border-orange-300 transition cursor-pointer overflow-hidden"
              onClick={() => { setSelected(f); setView("detail"); setDetailTab("info"); }}>
              <div className="px-4 py-3 flex items-start justify-between gap-2">
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
                    <span className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{f.styleName}</span>
                    <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{f.styleCode}</span>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{f.buyerName} • {f.fabricType} • {f.color}</p>
                </div>
                <Badge color={STATUS_COLORS[f.status] || "blue"} size="xs">{f.status}</Badge>
              </div>
              {/* Progress */}
              <div className="px-4 pb-2">
                <div className="flex justify-between text-xs text-gray-400 mb-1">
                  <span>{produced.toLocaleString()} / {f.orderQuantity.toLocaleString()} pcs</span>
                  <span className="font-bold text-orange-500">{progress}%</span>
                </div>
                <div className="w-full bg-gray-100 rounded-full h-1.5">
                  <div className="h-1.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: progress + "%", background: progress === 100 ? "#10B981" : "#F97316" }} />
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Footer */}
              <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-px bg-gray-100">
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{f.processes.length}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Processes</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs">{allEntries.filter(e => e.styleId === f.id).length}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Entries</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-white px-3 py-2 text-center">
                  <p className={"font-bold text-xs " + (daysLeft < 0 ? "text-red-500" : daysLeft < 7 ? "text-amber-500" : "text-green-600")}>
                    {daysLeft < 0 ? "Overdue" : daysLeft + "d"}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Delivery</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
        <Paginator page={sfPage} setPage={setSfPage} totalPages={sfTotalPages} total={sfTotal} pageSize={sfPageSize} />
      </div>

      {/* New Style Modal */}
      <Modal open={showStyleModal} onClose={() => { setShowStyleModal(false); setError(""); }} title="New Style File">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Style Code *" value={styleForm.styleCode} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, styleCode: e.target.value })} placeholder="SG-2024-005" />
            <Input label="Style Name *" value={styleForm.styleName} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, styleName: e.target.value })} placeholder="Men's Shirt" />
          </div>
          <Input label="Buyer Name *" value={styleForm.buyerName} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, buyerName: e.target.value })} placeholder="Reliance Retail" />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Fabric Type" value={styleForm.fabricType} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, fabricType: e.target.value })} placeholder="Cotton" />
            <Input label="Color" value={styleForm.color} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, color: e.target.value })} placeholder="White" />
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Size Range" value={styleForm.sizeRange} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, sizeRange: e.target.value })} placeholder="S-XXL" />
            <Input label="Order Qty *" type="number" value={styleForm.orderQuantity} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, orderQuantity: e.target.value })} placeholder="5000" />
          </div>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Delivery Date *" type="date" value={styleForm.deliveryDate} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, deliveryDate: e.target.value })} />
            <Select label="Status" value={styleForm.status} onChange={e => setStyleForm({ ...styleForm, status: e.target.value })}>
              {["Draft","Active","Completed","Closed"].map(s => <option key={s}>{s}</option>)}
            </Select>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowStyleModal(false); setError(""); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={addStyle} className="flex-1">Create Style File</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

const Styles = StyleFiles;


// OPERATIONS
const Operations = () => {
  const [ops, setOps] = useState(MOCK_DB.operations);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ name: "", nameHindi: "", pieceRate: "", department: "Stitching" });

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Operations / काम के प्रकार</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">Piece rate operations</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>+ Add Operation</Btn>
      </div>

      <Table
        headers={["Operation", "Hindi", "Department", "Piece Rate / दर", "Action"]}
        rows={ops.map(op => [
          <Td key="n"><span className="text-gray-900 font-medium">{op.name}</span></Td>,
          <Td key="h"><span className="text-gray-900">{op.nameHindi}</span></Td>,
          <Td key="d"><span className="text-sm px-2 py-1 rounded-full bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-400">{op.department}</span></Td>,
          <Td key="r"><span className="text-green-400 font-bold">₹{op.pieceRate.toFixed(2)}</span></Td>,
          <Td key="a">
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <button className="text-blue-400 hover:text-blue-300 text-xs">Edit</button>
              <button className="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 text-xs">Delete</button>
            </div>
          </Td>,
        ])}
      />

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)} title="Add Operation / नया काम">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Operation Name" value={form.name} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, name: e.target.value })} placeholder="Stitching" />
            <Input label="Hindi Name" labelHindi="हिंदी नाम" value={form.nameHindi} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, nameHindi: e.target.value })} placeholder="सिलाई" />
          </div>
          <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, department: e.target.value })}>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
          </Select>
          <Input label="Piece Rate (₹)" labelHindi="दर" type="number" step="0.01" value={form.pieceRate} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, pieceRate: e.target.value })} placeholder="2.50" />
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={() => { setOps([...ops, { ...form, id: `op${Date.now()}`, pieceRate: +form.pieceRate }]); setShowModal(false); }} className="flex-1">Add</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

  </div>
