// PAYMENTS — Auto Monthly Payment Report
const Payments = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const now = new Date();
  const MONTHS = [
    { label: "January 2024", value: "2024-01", closed: false },
    { label: "December 2023", value: "2023-12", closed: true },
    { label: "November 2023", value: "2023-11", closed: true },
  ];

  const [selectedMonth, setSelectedMonth] = useState("2024-01");
  const [payments, setPayments] = useState(MOCK_DB.payments);
  const [showSlip, setShowSlip] = useState(null);
  const [showCloseConfirm, setShowCloseConfirm] = useState(false);
  const [advanceModal, setAdvanceModal] = useState(null);
  const [advanceAmt, setAdvanceAmt] = useState("");

  const selectedMonthData = MONTHS.find(m => m.value === selectedMonth);
  const isClosed = selectedMonthData?.closed;

  // Auto-calculate from work entries (only verified ones)
  const WORK_ENTRIES_VERIFIED = MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e => ({ ...e, status: "verified" }));

  // Rule 10: Build payment report from verified work entries
  const buildReport = (monthKey) => {
    const [yr, mo] = monthKey.split("-").map(Number);
    // Group verified entries by worker
    const grouped = {};
    WORK_ENTRIES_VERIFIED.forEach(e => {
      const d = new Date(e.date);
      if (d.getFullYear() !== yr || d.getMonth() + 1 !== mo) return;
      if (!grouped[e.workerName]) {
        grouped[e.workerName] = {
          workerName: e.workerName, staffId: e.staffId, department: e.department,
          entries: [], totalQty: 0, grossAmount: 0,
        };
      }
      grouped[e.workerName].entries.push(e);
      grouped[e.workerName].totalQty += e.pieces;
      grouped[e.workerName].grossAmount += e.amount;
    });

    // Merge with payments data for deductions/status
    return Object.values(grouped).map(g => {
      const saved = payments.find(p => p.workerName === g.workerName);
      return {
        ...g,
        deductions: saved?.deductions || 0,
        advance: saved?.advance_deduction || 0,
        netAmount: g.grossAmount - (saved?.deductions || 0) - (saved?.advance_deduction || 0),
        status: saved?.status || "pending",
        id: saved?.id || `auto-${g.staffId}`,
      };
    });
  };

  const report = buildReport(selectedMonth);
  const totalQty = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.totalQty, 0);
  const totalGross = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.grossAmount, 0);
  const totalDeduct = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.deductions + r.advance, 0);
  const totalNet = report.reduce((s, r) => s + r.netAmount, 0);

  const markPaid = (id) => setPayments(payments.map(p => p.id === id ? { ...p, status: "paid" } : p));

  const exportCSV = () => {
    const rows = [
      ["Staff ID", "Worker Name", "Department", "Total Qty", "Gross Amount", "Deductions", "Net Amount", "Status"],
      ...report.map(r => [r.staffId, r.workerName, r.department, r.totalQty, r.grossAmount.toFixed(2), (r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(2), r.netAmount.toFixed(2), r.status]),
    ];
    const csv = rows.map(r => r.join(",")).join("\n");
    const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: "text/csv" });
    const a = document.createElement("a");
    a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    a.download = `payment-report-${selectedMonth}.csv`;
    a.click();
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Payment Report / भुगतान रिपोर्ट</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm">Verified entries से auto monthly report</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
          <select value={selectedMonth} onChange={e => setSelectedMonth(e.target.value)}
            className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
            {MONTHS.map(m => (
              <option key={m.value} value={m.value}>{m.label} {m.closed ? " [Closed]" : ""}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
          {user.role === "admin" && !isClosed && (
            <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(true)}>Close Month</Btn>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Month closed banner */}
      {isClosed && (
        <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-300 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
          <span className="text-2xl"></span>
          <div>
            <p className="text-red-800 font-bold text-sm">Month Closed / महीना बंद</p>
            <p className="text-red-600 text-xs">{selectedMonthData?.label} की entries lock हो चुकी हैं। कोई नई entry या बदलाव नहीं होगा।</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Rule 10 info */}
      <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl p-3">
        <p className="text-green-800 text-xs font-bold mb-1">Payment Report Rule (Rule 10):</p>
        <p className="text-green-700 text-xs">सिर्फ <strong>Verified</strong> work entries से auto payment calculate होती है। Pending entries payment में नहीं जाएंगी।</p>
      </div>

      {/* Summary cards */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-4 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Total Workers", value: report.length, color: "text-blue-600", bg: "bg-blue-50 border-blue-200" },
          { label: "Total Pieces", value: totalQty.toLocaleString(), color: "text-orange-600", bg: "bg-orange-50 border-orange-200" },
          { label: "Gross Amount", value: `₹${totalGross.toLocaleString()}`, color: "text-purple-600", bg: "bg-purple-50 border-purple-200" },
          { label: "Net Payable", value: `₹${totalNet.toLocaleString()}`, color: "text-green-600", bg: "bg-green-50 border-green-200" },
        ].map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className={`rounded-xl border-2 p-3 text-center ${s.bg}`}>
            <p className={`text-xl font-extrabold ${s.color}`}>{s.value}</p>
            <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Payment table */}
      <div className="space-y-3">
        {report.length === 0 && (
          <div className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400">इस month में कोई verified entry नहीं है।</div>
        )}
        {report.map((r, i) => (
          <div key={r.id || i} className={`bg-white rounded-2xl border-2 p-4 shadow-sm ${r.status === "paid" ? "border-green-200" : "border-gray-100"}`}>
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-500 to-orange-600 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-base shrink-0">
                  {r.workerName?.charAt(0)}
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{r.workerName}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{r.staffId} • {r.department}</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              <Badge color={r.status === "paid" ? "green" : r.status === "hold" ? "red" : "amber"} size="xs">
                {r.status === "paid" ? "Paid" : r.status === "hold" ? "Hold" : "Pending"}
              </Badge>
            </div>

            {/* Rule 10 breakdown table */}
            <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-xl p-3 mb-3">
              <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-bold mb-2">Auto Calculated — Verified Entries Only</p>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-center">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 font-extrabold text-base">{r.totalQty.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Total Qty</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-blue-600 font-bold text-base">₹{r.grossAmount.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Gross</p>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-red-500 font-bold text-base">-₹{(r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(0)}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Deduct</p>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-green-50 rounded-lg py-1">
                  <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-base">₹{r.netAmount.toLocaleString()}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Net Pay</p>
                </div>
              </div>
              {/* Formula reminder */}
              <p className="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs mt-2">
                Formula: {r.totalQty} pcs × avg rate = ₹{r.grossAmount.toFixed(0)} − ₹{(r.deductions + r.advance).toFixed(0)} = <strong className="text-green-600">₹{r.netAmount.toFixed(0)}</strong>
              </p>
            </div>

            {/* Entry breakdown (expand) */}
            {r.entries?.length > 0 && (
              <details className="mb-3">
                <summary className="text-xs text-blue-600 font-semibold cursor-pointer hover:text-blue-800">
                  {r.entries.length} verified entries देखें
                </summary>
                <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
                  {r.entries.map((e, j) => (
                    <div key={j} className="flex justify-between text-xs bg-gray-50 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5">
                      <span className="text-gray-700">{e.date} • {e.operation}</span>
                      <span className="text-gray-500">{e.pieces} × ₹{e.pieceRate}</span>
                      <span className="text-green-600 font-bold">₹{e.amount}</span>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </details>
            )}

            <div className="flex gap-2">
              {r.status !== "paid" && !isClosed && user.role !== "worker" && (
                <Btn variant="success" size="sm" className="flex-1 font-bold" onClick={() => markPaid(r.id)}>
                  Mark Paid
                </Btn>
              )}
              {r.status === "paid" && (
                <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-1 bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-xl py-2 text-green-600 text-xs font-bold">
                  ✓ Payment Done
                </div>
              )}
              <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" onClick={() => setShowSlip(r)}>Slip</Btn>
              {user.role !== "worker" && (
                <Btn variant="ghost" size="sm" className="border border-gray-200" onClick={() => { setAdvanceModal(r); setAdvanceAmt(""); }}>
                  Advance
                </Btn>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Export & Close */}
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={exportCSV}>Export CSV</Btn>
        {user.role === "admin" && !isClosed && (
          <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(true)}>Close Month & Lock</Btn>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Payment Slip Modal */}
      <Modal open={!!showSlip} onClose={() => setShowSlip(null)} title="Payment Slip / भुगतान पर्ची" size="sm">
        {showSlip && (
          <div className="space-y-3">
            <div className="border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded-xl p-4">
              <div className="text-center mb-3">
                <p className="font-extrabold text-gray-900 text-lg">Sharma Garments</p>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">Payment Slip — {selectedMonthData?.label}</p>
                <div className="border-t border-dashed border-gray-300 my-2" />
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-2 text-sm">
                {[
                  ["Worker", showSlip.workerName],
                  ["Staff ID", showSlip.staffId],
                  ["Department", showSlip.department],
                  ["Total Pieces", `${showSlip.totalQty} pcs`],
                  ["Gross Amount", `₹${showSlip.grossAmount.toFixed(2)}`],
                  ["Deductions", `-₹${(showSlip.deductions + showSlip.advance).toFixed(2)}`],
                ].map(([k, v]) => (
                  <div key={k} className="flex justify-between border-b border-gray-100 pb-1">
                    <span className="text-gray-500 font-semibold">{k}</span>
                    <span className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{v}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
                <div className="flex justify-between bg-green-50 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 mt-2">
                  <span className="text-green-700 font-extrabold">Net Payable / कुल</span>
                  <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-lg">₹{showSlip.netAmount.toFixed(2)}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="text-center mt-3 text-gray-400 text-xs">
                Status: <strong className={showSlip.status === "paid" ? "text-green-600" : "text-amber-600"}>{showSlip.status.toUpperCase()}</strong>
              </div>
            </div>
            <Btn className="w-full" onClick={() => window.print()}>Print Slip</Btn>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>

      {/* Advance Deduction Modal */}
      <Modal open={!!advanceModal} onClose={() => setAdvanceModal(null)} title="Advance Deduction" size="sm">
        {advanceModal && (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl p-3">
              <p className="text-amber-800 font-bold text-sm">{advanceModal.workerName}</p>
              <p className="text-amber-600 text-xs">Current Net: ₹{advanceModal.netAmount.toFixed(0)}</p>
            </div>
            <Input label="Advance Amount / अग्रिम राशि" type="number" value={advanceAmt} onChange={e => setAdvanceAmt(e.target.value)} placeholder="₹500" />
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setAdvanceModal(null)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn onClick={() => {
                setPayments(payments.map(p => p.workerName === advanceModal.workerName ? { ...p, advance_deduction: (p.advance_deduction || 0) + +advanceAmt } : p));
                setAdvanceModal(null);
              }} className="flex-1">Apply Deduction</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>

      {/* Close Month Confirm */}
      <Modal open={showCloseConfirm} onClose={() => setShowCloseConfirm(false)} title="Month Close करें?" size="sm">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <div className="bg-red-50 border-2 border-red-200 rounded-xl p-4">
            <p className="text-red-800 font-bold">Warning / चेतावनी</p>
            <p className="text-red-600 text-sm mt-1">{selectedMonthData?.label} को close करने के बाद:</p>
            <ul className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-2 space-y-1 list-disc list-inside">
              <li>कोई नई entry नहीं होगी</li>
              <li>Worker entries read-only हो जाएंगी</li>
              <li>सिर्फ Supervisor ही edit कर सकेगा</li>
              <li>यह action undo नहीं हो सकती</li>
            </ul>
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowCloseConfirm(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={() => { LOCKED_MONTHS.push(selectedMonth); setShowCloseConfirm(false); }} className="flex-1 bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600 text-white">
               Confirm Close
            </Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

// HOURLY REPORTS
const HourlyReports = () => {
  const [reports, setReports] = useState(MOCK_DB.hourlyReports);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ date: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0], department: "", style: "", hourSlot: "", total: "", pass: "", alter: "", reject: "" });

  const HOUR_SLOTS = ["08:00-09:00","09:00-10:00","10:00-11:00","11:00-12:00","12:00-13:00","14:00-15:00","15:00-16:00","16:00-17:00","17:00-18:00"];

  const handleAdd = () => {
    const total = +form.total;
    const pass = +form.pass;
    setReports([...reports, { ...form, id: `h${Date.now()}`, passPercent: total ? ((pass / total) * 100).toFixed(1) : 0 }]);
    setShowModal(false);
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Hourly Reports / घंटेवार रिपोर्ट</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">Production quality tracking</p>
        </div>
        <Btn onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>+ Add Report</Btn>
      </div>

      <div className="grid gap-3">
        {reports.map(r => (
          <div key={r.id} className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-4">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3 flex-wrap gap-2">
              <div>
                <span className="text-gray-900 font-semibold">{r.department}</span>
                <span className="text-gray-700 mx-2">•</span>
                <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{r.style}</span>
              </div>
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <span className="text-gray-700 text-sm">{r.hourSlot}</span>
                <span className={`font-bold text-sm px-3 py-1 rounded-full ${+r.passPercent >= 95 ? "bg-green-500/20 text-green-400" : +r.passPercent >= 90 ? "bg-amber-500/20 text-amber-400" : "bg-red-500/20 text-red-400"}`}>
                  {r.passPercent}% Pass
                </span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-center">
              {[
                { label: "Total", value: r.total, color: "text-gray-900" },
                { label: "Pass ✓", value: r.pass, color: "text-green-400" },
                { label: "Alter ↻", value: r.alter, color: "text-amber-400" },
                { label: "Reject ✗", value: r.reject, color: "text-red-400" },
              ].map(s => (
                <div key={s.label} className="bg-gray-100 rounded-xl p-2">
                  <p className={`text-xl font-bold ${s.color}`}>{s.value}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs">{s.label}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            {/* Pass bar */}
            <div className="mt-3">
              <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-1.5 flex overflow-hidden">
                <div className="h-full bg-green-500" style={{ width: `${(r.pass / r.total) * 100}%` }} />
                <div className="h-full bg-amber-500" style={{ width: `${(r.alter / r.total) * 100}%` }} />
                <div className="h-full bg-red-500" style={{ width: `${(r.reject / r.total) * 100}%` }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)} title="Hourly Report / घंटेवार रिपोर्ट">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          <Input label="Date" type="date" value={form.date} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, date: e.target.value })} />
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, department: e.target.value })}>
              <option value="">Select</option>
              {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <Select label="Style" value={form.style} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, style: e.target.value })}>
              <option value="">Select</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s => s.status === "active").map(s => <option key={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
            </Select>
          </div>
          <Select label="Hour Slot / समय" value={form.hourSlot} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, hourSlot: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">Select Hour</option>
            {HOUR_SLOTS.map(h => <option key={h}>{h}</option>)}
          </Select>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            <Input label="Total Pieces" type="number" value={form.total} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, total: e.target.value })} />
            <Input label="Pass Pieces ✓" type="number" value={form.pass} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, pass: e.target.value })} />
            <Input label="Alter Pieces ↻" type="number" value={form.alter} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, alter: e.target.value })} />
            <Input label="Reject Pieces ✗" type="number" value={form.reject} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, reject: e.target.value })} />
          </div>
          {form.total && form.pass && (
            <div className="bg-green-500/10 border border-green-500/20 rounded-xl p-3 text-center">
              <span className="text-green-400 font-bold text-xl">
                {((+form.pass / +form.total) * 100).toFixed(1)}% Pass Rate
              </span>
            </div>
          )}
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setShowModal(false)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={handleAdd} className="flex-1">Submit Report</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};

// SELF / DEMO ENTRY — Worker submits, Supervisor verifies


// JOB PORTAL
const JobPortal = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [jobs, setJobs] = useState(MOCK_DB.jobs);
  const [showModal, setShowModal] = useState(false);
  const [applyModal, setApplyModal] = useState(null);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ title: "", department: "", salary: "", experience: "", openings: "1", description: "", workType: "" });
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  const emptyForm = { title: "", department: "", salary: "", experience: "", openings: "1", description: "", workType: "" };

  const postJob = () => {
    if (!form.title || !form.department) { setError("Job Title और Department जरूरी है।"); return; }
    const newJob = {
      id: "j" + Date.now(),
      title: form.title,
      department: form.department,
      salary: form.salary || "Not specified",
      experience: form.experience || "Any",
      openings: +form.openings || 1,
      description: form.description,
      workType: form.workType,
      status: "active",
      postedDate: new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0],
      applications: 0,
    };
    setJobs([newJob, ...jobs]);
    setShowModal(false);
    setForm(emptyForm);
    setError("");
  };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between flex-wrap gap-3">
        <div>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Job Portal / नौकरी</h1>
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{jobs.filter(j => j.status === "active").length} active openings</p>
        </div>
        {(user.role === "admin" || user.role === "supervisor") && (
          <Btn onClick={() => setShowModal(true)}>+ Post Job</Btn>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        {jobs.map(job => (
          <div key={job.id} className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-5 hover:border-orange-500/30 transition">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between mb-3">
              <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-500/20 to-blue-600/20 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-2xl border border-blue-500/20">
                Dept
              </div>
              <Badge color={job.status === "active" ? "green" : "slate"} size="xs">{job.status}</Badge>
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-bold">{job.title}</h3>
            <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm mt-0.5">{job.department} Department</p>
            {job.workType && (
              <span className={"inline-block mt-1 text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-lg " +
                (job.workType === "salary" ? "bg-blue-50 text-blue-700" :
                 job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "bg-orange-50 text-orange-600" :
                 "bg-green-50 text-green-700")}>
                {job.workType === "salary" ? "Salary Based" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "Piece Rate" : "Commission"}
              </span>
            )}
            <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs mt-2">{job.description}</p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 mt-3 text-xs">
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Work Type</p>
                <p className={"font-semibold " + (job.workType === "salary" ? "text-blue-600" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "text-orange-500" : "text-green-600")}>
                  {job.workType === "salary" ? "Salary" : job.workType === "piece_rate" ? "Piece Rate" : job.workType === "commission" ? "Commission" : "—"}
                </p>
              </div>
              {job.workType === "salary" && (
                <div className="bg-blue-50 rounded-lg p-2">
                  <p className="text-gray-900">Salary</p>
                  <p className="text-blue-700 font-extrabold">{job.salary}</p>
                </div>
              )}
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Experience</p>
                <p className="text-blue-400 font-semibold">{job.experience}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-gray-100 rounded-lg p-2">
                <p className="text-gray-900">Kitne Workers Chahiye</p>
                <p className="text-orange-400 font-bold">{job.openings}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2 mt-3">
              {user.role === "worker" || user.role === "contractor" ? (
                <Btn onClick={() => setApplyModal(job)} className="flex-1">Apply Now</Btn>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <Btn variant="secondary" size="sm" className="flex-1">View Applications</Btn>
                  <Btn variant="danger" size="sm">Close</Btn>
                </>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <Modal open={showModal} onClose={() => setShowModal(false)} title="Post New Job / नौकरी पोस्ट करें">
        <div className="space-y-4">
          {error && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-700 text-sm font-semibold">{error}</div>}
          <Input label="Job Title" value={form.title} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, title: e.target.value })} placeholder="Experienced Tailor" />
          <Select label="Department" value={form.department} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, department: e.target.value })}>
            <option value="">Select Department</option>
            {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
          </Select>

          {/* Work Type Cards */}
          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-bold text-gray-900 mb-2">Work Type / काम का प्रकार</label>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
              {[
                { key: "salary",     label: "Salary",      hindi: "मासिक वेतन", icon: "jobs", color: "blue"   },
                { key: "piece_rate", label: "Piece Rate",  hindi: "पीस रेट",    icon: "", color: "orange" },
                { key: "commission", label: "Commission",  hindi: "कमीशन",      icon: "", color: "green"  },
              ].map(t => (
                <button key={t.key} type="button"
                  onClick={() => setForm({ ...form, workType: t.key })}
                  className={"rounded-2xl border-2 p-3 text-center transition " +
                    (form.workType === t.key
                      ? t.color === "blue"   ? "border-blue-500 bg-blue-50"
                      : t.color === "orange" ? "border-orange-500 bg-orange-50"
                      :                        "border-green-500 bg-green-50"
                      : "border-gray-200 bg-white hover:border-gray-300")}>
                  <div className="text-2xl mb-1">{t.icon}</div>
                  <p className={"text-xs font-extrabold " +
                    (form.workType === t.key
                      ? t.color === "blue" ? "text-blue-700" : t.color === "orange" ? "text-orange-600" : "text-green-700"
                      : "text-gray-700")}>
                    {t.label}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{t.hindi}</p>
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Salary field — only when Salary type selected */}
          {form.workType === "salary" && (
            <div className="bg-blue-50 border-2 border-blue-200 rounded-2xl p-3 space-y-3">
              <p className="text-blue-700 text-xs font-extrabold">Salary Details</p>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                <Input label="Min Salary (Rs)" type="number" value={form.salaryMin || ""} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salaryMin: e.target.value, salary: `Rs ${e.target.value}${form.salaryMax ? " - Rs " + form.salaryMax : ""}` })} placeholder="8000" />
                <Input label="Max Salary (Rs)" type="number" value={form.salaryMax || ""} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salaryMax: e.target.value, salary: `Rs ${form.salaryMin || ""}${e.target.value ? " - Rs " + e.target.value : ""}` })} placeholder="12000" />
              </div>
              {form.salaryMin && (
                <div className="bg-white rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-sm">
                  <span className="text-gray-500">Salary Range: </span>
                  <span className="text-blue-700 font-extrabold">Rs {form.salaryMin}{form.salaryMax ? " - Rs " + form.salaryMax : "+"} / month</span>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
            {form.workType !== "salary" && (
              <Input label="Salary Range" value={form.salary} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, salary: e.target.value })} placeholder="Rs 8,000-12,000" />
            )}
            <Input label="Experience" value={form.experience} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, experience: e.target.value })} placeholder="2+ years" className={form.workType === "salary" ? "" : ""} />
          </div>
          <Input label="Kitne Workers Chahiye" type="number" value={form.openings} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, openings: e.target.value })} />
          <div className="space-y-1.5">
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Description</label>
            <textarea value={form.description} onChange={e => setForm({ ...form, description: e.target.value })}
              rows={3} placeholder="Job description..."
              className="w-full bg-white border border-slate-600 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500 placeholder-slate-400" />
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3">
            <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => { setShowModal(false); setError(""); setForm(emptyForm); }} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn onClick={postJob} className="flex-1">Post Job</Btn>
          </div>
        </div>
      </Modal>

      <Modal open={!!applyModal} onClose={() => setApplyModal(null)} title="Apply for Job / आवेदन करें">
        {applyModal && (
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <div className="bg-blue-500/10 border border-blue-500/20 rounded-xl p-3">
              <p className="text-blue-400 font-semibold">{applyModal.title}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm">{applyModal.department} • {applyModal.salary}</p>
            </div>
            <Input label="Your Name" placeholder="Full name" />
            <Input label="Mobile Number" type="tel" placeholder="Your mobile" />
            <Input label="Experience (years)" type="number" placeholder="2" />
            <Input label="Expected Salary" placeholder="₹10,000" />
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Skills / कौशल</label>
              <textarea rows={2} placeholder="Stitching, Overlock, etc."
                className="w-full bg-white border border-slate-600 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500 placeholder-slate-400" />
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" onClick={() => setApplyModal(null)} className="flex-1">Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn onClick={() => setApplyModal(null)} className="flex-1">Submit Application</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
};


// PROFILE
const Profile = ({ onLogout }) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [prof, setProf] = useState({
    name:     user.name,
    mobile:   user.mobile,
    email:    "raj@sharmagarments.com",
    factory:  user.tenantName || "Sharma Garments Pvt Ltd",
    location: "Ludhiana, Punjab",
    language: "Hindi",
  });
  const [editMode,    setEditMode]    = useState(false);
  const [draft,       setDraft]       = useState(prof);
  const [profSaved,   setProfSaved]   = useState(false);

  const saveProf = () => { setProf(draft); setEditMode(false); setProfSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setProfSaved(false),2500); };

  const field = (label, key, type="text", opts=null) => (
    <div key={key} className="flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0 gap-3">
      <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm shrink-0">{label}</span>
      {editMode ? (
        opts ? (
          <select value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(d=>({...d,[key]:e.target.value}))}
            className="bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500 text-right" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
            {opts.map(o=><option key={o}>{o}</option>)}
          </select>
        ) : (
          <input type={type} value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(d=>({...d,[key]:e.target.value}))}
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold text-right focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-500" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
        )
      ) : (
        <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold text-right">{prof[key] || "—"}</span>
      )}
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Profile / प्रोफाइल</h1>

      {profSaved && (
        <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
          <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
            <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </div>
          <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Profile save हो गई!</p>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Avatar */}
      <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 p-6 text-center">
        <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-500 to-orange-600 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white text-3xl font-bold mx-auto mb-3 shadow-lg shadow-orange-500/30">
          {prof.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
        </div>
        <h2 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">{prof.name}</h2>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-0.5">{prof.mobile}</p>
        <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <Badge color={user.role==="admin"?"purple":user.role==="supervisor"?"blue":"green"}>
            {user.role.toUpperCase()}
          </Badge>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Edit / Save */}
      <div className="flex gap-2">
        {editMode ? (
          <>
            <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>{setEditMode(false);setDraft(prof);}}>Cancel</Btn>
            <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={saveProf}>Save Changes</Btn>
          </>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(true);setDraft(prof);}}
            className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 bg-white border-2 border-orange-400 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
            <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            Edit Profile
          </button>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Editable fields */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 px-5 py-2 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider pt-3 pb-1">Personal Info {editMode && <span className="text-orange-400">— Editing</span>}</p>
        {field("Name / नाम",         "name")}
        {field("Mobile / मोबाइल",    "mobile",   "tel")}
        {field("Email",               "email",    "email")}
        {field("Language",            "language", "text", ["Hindi","English","Hindi + English"])}
      </div>

      {/* Factory info */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 px-5 py-2 shadow-sm">
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider pt-3 pb-1">Factory Info</p>
        {field("Factory Name",   "factory")}
        {field("Location / पता", "location")}
        {[
          { label:"Total Workers", value:"31 Active" },
          { label:"Plan",          value:"Pro Plan"   },
        ].map(item=>(
          <div key={item.label} className="flex justify-between py-3 border-b border-gray-100 last:border-0">
            <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{item.label}</span>
            <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{item.value}</span>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <Btn variant="danger" className="w-full" size="lg" onClick={onLogout}>
        Sign Out / लॉगआउट
      </Btn>
    </div>
  );
};

// EXPORT CENTER
const ExportCenter = () => {
  const [dateFrom, setDateFrom] = useState("");
  const [dateTo,   setDateTo]   = useState("");
  const [dept,     setDept]     = useState("all");
  const [done,     setDone]     = useState("");

  const flash = (label) => { setDone(label); setTimeout(() => setDone(""), 2500); };

  const downloadCSV = (filename, headers, rows) => {
    const esc = (v) => '"' + String(v ?? "").replace(/"/g, '""') + '"';
    const csv = [headers.map(esc).join(","), ...rows.map(r => r.map(esc).join(","))].join("\r\n");
    const blob = new Blob(["\uFEFF" + csv], { type: "text/csv;charset=utf-8;" });
    const url  = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a    = document.createElement("a");
    a.href = url; a.download = filename; a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  };

  const inRange = (d) => {
    if (dateFrom && d < dateFrom) return false;
    if (dateTo   && d > dateTo)   return false;
    return true;
  };

  const exportWorkEntries = () => {
    const rows = MOCK_DB.workEntries
      .filter(e => inRange(e.date) && (dept === "all" || e.department === dept))
      .map(e => [e.date, e.workerName, e.staffId, e.department, e.styleName, e.operation, e.pieces, e.pieceRate, e.amount, e.status || "verified"]);
    if (!rows.length) { alert("No data for selected filters."); return; }
    downloadCSV("work-entries.csv", ["Date","Worker","Staff ID","Dept","Style","Operation","Pieces","Rate","Amount","Status"], rows);
    flash("Work Entries");
  };
  const exportWorkers = () => {
    const rows = MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => dept === "all" || w.department === dept)
      .map(w => [w.staffId, w.name, w.mobile, w.department, w.joinDate, w.status]);
    downloadCSV("workers.csv", ["Staff ID","Name","Mobile","Department","Join Date","Status"], rows);
    flash("Workers");
  };
  const exportPayments = () => {
    const rows = MOCK_DB.payments.filter(p => dept === "all" || p.department === dept)
      .map(p => [p.workerName, p.staffId, p.department, p.month, p.totalPieces, p.grossAmount, p.deductions, p.netAmount, p.status]);
    downloadCSV("payments.csv", ["Worker","Staff ID","Dept","Month","Pieces","Gross","Deductions","Net","Status"], rows);
    flash("Payments");
  };
  const exportHourly = () => {
    const rows = MOCK_DB.hourlyReports.filter(h => inRange(h.date) && (dept === "all" || h.department === dept))
      .map(h => [h.date, h.department, h.style, h.hourSlot, h.total, h.pass, h.alter, h.reject, h.passPercent]);
    if (!rows.length) { alert("No data for selected filters."); return; }
    downloadCSV("hourly-reports.csv", ["Date","Dept","Style","Slot","Total","Pass","Alter","Reject","Pass%"], rows);
    flash("Hourly Reports");
  };
  const exportStyles = () => {
    const rows = MOCK_DB.styles.map(s => [s.styleNumber, s.styleName, s.buyer, s.totalQuantity, s.completedQty, Math.round((s.completedQty / s.totalQuantity) * 100), s.status, s.targetDate]);
    downloadCSV("styles.csv", ["Style No","Style Name","Buyer","Total Qty","Completed","Progress%","Status","Target Date"], rows);
    flash("Styles");
  };

  const CARDS = [
    { id: "work",    icon: "W", title: "Work Entries",   count: MOCK_DB.workEntries.length,   color: "orange", onExport: exportWorkEntries, dateFilter: true,  deptFilter: true  },
    { id: "workers", icon: "workers", title: "Workers",        count: MOCK_DB.workers.length,        color: "blue",   onExport: exportWorkers,     dateFilter: false, deptFilter: true  },
    { id: "pay",     icon: "P", title: "Payments",       count: MOCK_DB.payments.length,       color: "green",  onExport: exportPayments,    dateFilter: false, deptFilter: true  },
    { id: "hourly",  icon: "hourly", title: "Hourly Reports", count: MOCK_DB.hourlyReports.length,  color: "purple", onExport: exportHourly,      dateFilter: true,  deptFilter: true  },
    { id: "styles",  icon: "styles", title: "Styles / Orders",count: MOCK_DB.styles.length,         color: "amber",  onExport: exportStyles,      dateFilter: false, deptFilter: false },
  ];

  const btnStyle = { orange: "bg-orange-500 text-white", blue: "bg-blue-500 text-white", green: "bg-green-500 text-white", purple: "bg-purple-500 text-white", amber: "bg-amber-500 text-white" };
  const bgStyle  = { orange: "border-orange-200 bg-orange-50", blue: "border-blue-200 bg-blue-50", green: "border-green-200 bg-green-50", purple: "border-purple-200 bg-purple-50", amber: "border-amber-200 bg-amber-50" };

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6">
      {done && (
        <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-6 py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-2xl font-bold text-sm">
          {done} exported successfully!
        </div>
      )}

      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Export Center</h1>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-0.5">Download factory data as CSV files</p>
      </div>

      <div className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl p-4">
        <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wide mb-3">Filters</p>
        <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-3 gap-3">
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-700">From Date</label>
            <input type="date" value={dateFrom} onChange={e => setDateFrom(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"
              style={{ fontSize: "16px" }} />
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-700">To Date</label>
            <input type="date" value={dateTo} onChange={e => setDateTo(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"
              style={{ fontSize: "16px" }} />
          </div>
          <div className="space-y-1">
            <label className="block text-xs font-bold text-gray-700">Department</label>
            <select value={dept} onChange={e => setDept(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400"
              style={{ fontSize: "16px" }}>
              <option value="all">All Departments</option>
              {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
            </select>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="grid sm:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        {CARDS.map(c => (
          <div key={c.id} className={"border-2 rounded-2xl p-5 space-y-3 " + bgStyle[c.color]}>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <span className="text-2xl">{c.icon}</span>
              <div>
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{c.title}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{c.count} records</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2 text-xs">
              <span className={"px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium border " + (c.dateFilter ? "border-green-300 text-green-700 bg-white" : "border-gray-200 text-gray-400 bg-white")}>
                {c.dateFilter ? "Date filter" : "No date filter"}
              </span>
              <span className={"px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full font-medium border " + (c.deptFilter ? "border-green-300 text-green-700 bg-white" : "border-gray-200 text-gray-400 bg-white")}>
                {c.deptFilter ? "Dept filter" : "No dept filter"}
              </span>
            </div>
            <button onClick={c.onExport} className={"w-full py-3 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold active:scale-95 transition " + btnStyle[c.color]}>
              Download CSV
            </button>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="bg-gray-900 rounded-2xl p-5 flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-center gap-4">
        <div className="flex-1">
          <p className="text-white font-extrabold">Export Everything</p>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">Downloads all 5 reports as separate CSV files</p>
        </div>
        <button onClick={() => { exportWorkEntries(); setTimeout(exportWorkers, 400); setTimeout(exportPayments, 800); setTimeout(exportHourly, 1200); setTimeout(exportStyles, 1600); }}
          className="w-full sm:w-auto bg-orange-500 hover:bg-orange-600 active:scale-95 text-white font-bold px-6 py-3 rounded-xl transition text-sm shrink-0">
          Export All (5 files)
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// ============================================================
// STAFF PAYMENT — Full Details
// ============================================================
const StaffPaymentFull = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [workers]       = useState(MOCK_DB.workers);
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [deptFilter, setDeptFilter] = useState("all");
  const [statusFilter, setStatusFilter] = useState("all");
  const [selectedWorker, setSelectedWorker] = useState(null);
  const [showSlip, setShowSlip]   = useState(false);
  const [toast, setToast]         = useState("");
  const [payStatus, setPayStatus] = useState({}); // workerID -> "paid"|"pending"

  const flash = (m) => { setToast(m); setTimeout(() => setToast(""), 2500); };

  // Build per-worker payment from work entries
  const workerPayments = workers.map(w => {
    const entries = MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e => e.workerId === w.id && e.status === "verified");
    const totalPieces = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.pieces, 0);
    const grossAmount = entries.reduce((s, e) => s + e.amount, 0);
    const deductions  = MOCK_DB.payments.find(p => p.workerId === w.id)?.deductions || 0;
    const advance     = MOCK_DB.payments.find(p => p.workerId === w.id)?.advance_deduction || 0;
    const netAmount   = grossAmount - deductions - advance;
    const status      = payStatus[w.id] || (MOCK_DB.payments.find(p => p.workerId === w.id)?.status || "pending");
    return { ...w, entries, totalPieces, grossAmount, deductions, advance, netAmount, status };
  });

  const filtered = workerPayments
    .filter(w => deptFilter === "all" || w.department === deptFilter)
    .filter(w => statusFilter === "all" || w.status === statusFilter)
    .filter(w => !search || w.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()) || w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase()));

  const totalPieces = filtered.reduce((s, w) => s + w.totalPieces, 0);
  const totalGross  = filtered.reduce((s, w) => s + w.grossAmount, 0);
  const totalNet    = filtered.reduce((s, w) => s + w.netAmount, 0);
  const paidCount   = filtered.filter(w => w.status === "paid").length;

  const { paged: pagedWorkers, page: wpPage, setPage: setWpPage, totalPages: wpTotal, total: wpTotalCount, pageSize: wpPageSize } = usePagination(filtered, 20);

  const markPaid = (id) => { setPayStatus(p => ({ ...p, [id]: "paid" })); flash("Payment Marked Paid!"); };

  // Detail view
  if (selectedWorker) {
    const w = workerPayments.find(x => x.id === selectedWorker);
    return (
      <div className="space-y-4">
        {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <button onClick={() => setSelectedWorker(null)} className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 text-orange-600 text-sm font-bold">← Back</button>
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-lg font-extrabold text-gray-900">{w.name}</h1>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} • {w.department}</p>
          </div>
          <Badge color={w.status === "paid" ? "green" : "amber"} size="xs" className="ml-auto">
            {w.status === "paid" ? "Paid" : "Pending"}
          </Badge>
        </div>

        {/* Summary */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
          {[
            { label: "Total Pieces", value: w.totalPieces + " pcs", color: "text-orange-600", bg: "bg-orange-50 border-orange-200" },
            { label: "Gross Amount", value: "Rs " + w.grossAmount.toLocaleString(), color: "text-blue-600", bg: "bg-blue-50 border-blue-200" },
            { label: "Deductions",   value: "- Rs " + (w.deductions + w.advance), color: "text-red-500", bg: "bg-red-50 border-red-200" },
            { label: "Net Payable",  value: "Rs " + w.netAmount.toLocaleString(), color: "text-green-600", bg: "bg-green-50 border-green-200" },
          ].map(s => (
            <div key={s.label} className={"rounded-2xl border-2 p-3 text-center " + s.bg}>
              <p className={"text-xl font-extrabold " + s.color}>{s.value}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Formula */}
        <div className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-sm text-center text-gray-600">
          Formula: <span className="font-bold text-orange-500">{w.totalPieces} pcs</span> × avg rate = <span className="font-bold text-blue-600">Rs {w.grossAmount}</span> − <span className="font-bold text-red-500">Rs {w.deductions + w.advance}</span> = <span className="font-extrabold text-green-600 text-base">Rs {w.netAmount}</span>
        </div>

        {/* Entry breakdown */}
        <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
          <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
            <div>Date</div>
            <div>Operation</div>
            <div className="text-center">Pieces</div>
            <div className="text-right">Amount</div>
          </div>
          {w.entries.length === 0 && <p className="text-center py-8 text-gray-400 text-sm">No verified entries</p>}
          {w.entries.map((e, i) => (
            <div key={e.id} className={"grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-3 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/40")}>
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{e.date}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-800 text-xs font-semibold">{e.operation}</span>
              <span className="text-center text-orange-500 font-extrabold text-sm">{e.pieces}</span>
              <span className="text-right text-green-600 font-bold text-sm">Rs {e.amount}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
          {w.entries.length > 0 && (
            <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-4 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold">
              <div className="col-span-2 text-gray-300">TOTAL</div>
              <div className="text-center text-orange-400">{w.totalPieces} pcs</div>
              <div className="text-right text-green-400">Rs {w.grossAmount}</div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Actions */}
        <div className="flex gap-3">
          {w.status !== "paid" && user.role !== "worker" && (
            <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={() => { markPaid(w.id); setSelectedWorker(null); }}>Mark as Paid</Btn>
          )}
          {w.status === "paid" && (
            <div className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center bg-green-50 border-2 border-green-200 rounded-xl py-2.5 text-green-600 font-bold text-sm">Payment Done</div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Salary Slip — table */}
        <div className="border-2 border-dashed border-gray-300 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden bg-white">
          {/* Header */}
          <div className="bg-gray-800 px-4 py-3 text-center">
            <p className="font-extrabold text-white text-sm tracking-widest uppercase">SHARMA GARMENTS</p>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">SALARY SLIP / वेतन पर्ची</p>
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{new Date().toLocaleDateString("en-IN", { day:"2-digit", month:"short", year:"numeric" })}</p>
          </div>
          {/* Table rows */}
          {[
            ["Worker Name",   w.name],
            ["Staff ID",      w.staffId],
            ["Department",    w.department],
            ["Mobile",        w.mobile],
            ["Total Pieces",  w.totalPieces + " pcs"],
            ["Gross Amount",  "Rs " + w.grossAmount],
            ["Deductions",    "Rs " + (w.deductions + w.advance)],
          ].map(([k, v], i) => (
            <div key={k} className={"flex justify-between px-4 py-2.5 border-b border-gray-100 " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/50")}>
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{k}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{v}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
          {/* Net Payable */}
          <div className="flex justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-green-50 border-t-2 border-green-200">
            <span className="text-gray-800 font-extrabold text-sm">NET PAYABLE / कुल देय</span>
            <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-base">Rs {w.netAmount}</span>
          </div>
          {/* Status */}
          <div className="flex justify-between px-4 py-2.5 bg-gray-50">
            <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">Status</span>
            <span className={"font-extrabold text-sm " + (w.status === "paid" ? "text-green-600" : "text-amber-500")}>{w.status.toUpperCase()}</span>
          </div>
          <div className="text-center py-2 text-xs text-gray-300 border-t border-gray-100">* Computer generated slip *</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // List view
  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {toast && <div className="fixed top-16 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 z-50 bg-green-500 text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-2xl shadow-xl font-bold text-sm">{toast}</div>}

      <div>
        <h1 className="text-xl font-extrabold text-gray-900">Staff Payment</h1>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">Worker-wise full payment details</p>
      </div>

      {/* Summary pills */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
        {[
          { label: "Total Pieces", value: totalPieces.toLocaleString() + " pcs", color: "text-orange-600", bg: "bg-orange-50 border-orange-200" },
          { label: "Net Payable",  value: "Rs " + totalNet.toLocaleString(), color: "text-green-600", bg: "bg-green-50 border-green-200" },
          { label: "Paid",         value: paidCount + " / " + filtered.length, color: "text-blue-600", bg: "bg-blue-50 border-blue-200" },
          { label: "Gross Total",  value: "Rs " + totalGross.toLocaleString(), color: "text-purple-600", bg: "bg-purple-50 border-purple-200" },
        ].map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className={"rounded-xl border-2 px-3 py-2.5 text-center " + s.bg}>
            <p className={"text-base font-extrabold " + s.color}>{s.value}</p>
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{s.label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Filters */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
        <input value={search} onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)} placeholder="Search name / ID..."
          className="flex-1 min-w-[140px] bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400" />
        <select value={deptFilter} onChange={e => setDeptFilter(e.target.value)}
          className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-700 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
          <option value="all">All Depts</option>
          {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d => <option key={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
        </select>
        <select value={statusFilter} onChange={e => setStatusFilter(e.target.value)}
          className="bg-white border-2 border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-700 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:border-orange-400">
          <option value="all">All Status</option>
          <option value="pending">Pending</option>
          <option value="paid">Paid</option>
        </select>
      </div>

      {/* Worker payment table */}
      <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 overflow-hidden">
        {/* Table header */}
        <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-6 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold text-white uppercase tracking-wide">
          <div className="col-span-4">Worker</div>
          <div className="col-span-1 text-right">Net Pay</div>
          <div className="col-span-1 text-right">Status</div>
        </div>

        {filtered.length === 0 && (
          <p className="text-center py-10 text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
        )}

        {pagedWorkers.map((w, i) => (
          <div key={w.id}
            className={"grid grid-cols-6 px-4 py-3 items-center border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0 cursor-pointer hover:bg-orange-50/40 transition " + (i % 2 === 0 ? "bg-white" : "bg-gray-50/30")}
            onClick={() => setSelectedWorker(w.id)}>
            <div className="col-span-4 flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
              <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-lg bg-orange-100 flex items-center justify-center font-extrabold text-orange-600 text-xs shrink-0">
                {w.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-xs truncate">{w.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="col-span-1 text-right">
              <span className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {w.netAmount}</span>
            </div>
            <div className="col-span-1 text-right">
              <span className={"text-xs font-bold " + (w.status === "paid" ? "text-green-600" : "text-amber-500")}>
                {w.status === "paid" ? "✓" : "•"}
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}

        {filtered.length > 0 && (
          <div className="bg-gray-800 grid grid-cols-6 px-4 py-2.5 text-xs font-extrabold">
            <div className="col-span-4 text-gray-300">TOTAL ({filtered.length})</div>
            <div className="col-span-1 text-right text-green-400">Rs {totalNet}</div>
            <div className="col-span-1"></div>
          </div>
        )}
        <Paginator page={wpPage} setPage={setWpPage} totalPages={wpTotal} total={wpTotalCount} pageSize={wpPageSize} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

// SUPERVISOR PANEL — 5-Tab Dedicated Shell
// ============================================================
// ── Add Member by ID lookup ──
const AddMemberById = ({ myTeam, onAdd, onClose, TODAY }) => {
  const [idInput,  setIdInput]  = useState("");
  const [found,    setFound]    = useState(null);  // matched worker
  const [notFound, setNotFound] = useState(false);
  const [manualMode, setManualMode] = useState(false);
  const [manual, setManual] = useState({ name:"", mobile:"", department:"", staffId:"", joinDate:TODAY });
  const [manErr, setManErr] = useState("");

  // All workers in system (active + inactive) — pool to search from
  const POOL = [
    ...MOCK_DB.workers,
    { id:"w7", name:"Ajay Sharma",   staffId:"SG007", mobile:"9871234567", department:"Cutting",    joinDate:"2023-06-01", status:"inactive" },
    { id:"w8", name:"Kavita Yadav",  staffId:"SG008", mobile:"9882345678", department:"Finishing",  joinDate:"2023-09-15", status:"inactive" },
    { id:"w9", name:"Deepak Verma",  staffId:"SG009", mobile:"9893456789", department:"Stitching",  joinDate:"2024-01-02", status:"inactive" },
    { id:"w10",name:"Seema Patel",   staffId:"SG010", mobile:"9804567890", department:"Embroidery", joinDate:"2024-01-10", status:"inactive" },
  ];

  const alreadyInTeam = (w) => myTeam.some(m => m.id === w.id || m.staffId === w.staffId);

  const handleSearch = (val) => {
    setIdInput(val);
    setNotFound(false);
    setFound(null);
    if (val.trim().length < 2) return;
    const q = val.trim().toLowerCase();
    const match = POOL.find(w =>
      w.staffId.toLowerCase() === q ||
      w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      w.mobile === q
    );
    if (match) { setFound(match); }
    else if (val.trim().length >= 4) { setNotFound(true); }
  };

  const DEPT_COLOR = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };

  if (manualMode) return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      <button onClick={()=>{setManualMode(false);setManErr("");}}
        className="flex items-center gap-1 text-blue-500 font-bold text-sm mb-2">
        <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
        ID Search पर वापस
      </button>
      {manErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{manErr}</div>}
      <Input label="Full Name / नाम" value={manual.name} placeholder="Worker का पूरा नाम"
        onChange={e=>setManual(m=>({...m,name:e.target.value}))}/>
      <Input label="Mobile / मोबाइल" type="tel" value={manual.mobile} placeholder="10 digit"
        onChange={e=>setManual(m=>({...m,mobile:e.target.value}))}/>
      <Select label="Department" value={manual.department} onChange={e=>setManual(m=>({...m,department:e.target.value}))}>
        <option value="">-- Department चुनें --</option>
        {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=><option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
      </Select>
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
        <Input label="Staff ID" value={manual.staffId} placeholder="SG011"
          onChange={e=>setManual(m=>({...m,staffId:e.target.value}))}/>
        <Input label="Join Date" type="date" value={manual.joinDate} max={TODAY}
          onChange={e=>setManual(m=>({...m,joinDate:e.target.value}))}/>
      </div>
      <div className="flex gap-3">
        <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={onClose}>Cancel</Btn>
        <Btn className="flex-1 bg-blue-500" onClick={()=>{
          if (!manual.name.trim())              { setManErr("नाम जरूरी है।"); return; }
          if (!/^\d{10}$/.test(manual.mobile)) { setManErr("10 अंकों का mobile डालें।"); return; }
          if (!manual.department)               { setManErr("Department चुनें।"); return; }
          onAdd({ id:"w"+Date.now(), ...manual, staffId:manual.staffId||("SG0"+(myTeam.length+11)) });
        }}>Add Member →</Btn>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="space-y-5">
      {/* ID input */}
      <div>
        <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-semibold mb-2">Worker का Staff ID या Mobile डालें</p>
        <div className="relative">
          <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
            <rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="16" rx="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/>
            <path d="M7 8h10M7 12h7M7 16h5" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/>
          </svg>
          <input
            autoFocus
            value={idInput}
            onChange={e=>handleSearch(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="जैसे SG006 या 9867890123..."
            className="w-full bg-gray-50 border-2 border-blue-300 rounded-2xl pl-11 pr-4 py-3.5 text-gray-900 font-bold text-base focus:outline-none focus:border-blue-500 transition"
            style={{fontSize:"16px"}}
          />
          {idInput && (
            <button onClick={()=>{setIdInput("");setFound(null);setNotFound(false);}}
              className="absolute right-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400 active:text-gray-600">
              <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Quick suggestions */}
      {!idInput && (
        <div>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Available Workers</p>
          <div className="space-y-2 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto">
            {POOL.filter(w=>!alreadyInTeam(w)).map(w=>(
              <button key={w.id} onClick={()=>setFound(w)}
                className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 bg-gray-50 hover:bg-blue-50 border border-gray-100 hover:border-blue-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 transition text-left active:scale-[0.98]">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-sm shrink-0"
                  style={{background:DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B"}}>
                  {w.name.charAt(0)}
                </div>
                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{w.name}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-blue-500 text-xs font-bold shrink-0">Tap to add</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Found result */}
      {found && (
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <div className={`rounded-2xl border-2 overflow-hidden ${alreadyInTeam(found)?"border-gray-200":"border-blue-400"}`}>
            <div className="px-1 py-1" style={{background:DEPT_COLOR[found.department]||"#64748B"}}>
              <p className="text-white text-xs font-bold text-center py-0.5">{found.department}</p>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-4 bg-white">
              <div className="w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white text-2xl font-black shrink-0"
                style={{background:DEPT_COLOR[found.department]||"#64748B"}}>
                {found.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="flex-1">
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-base">{found.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{found.staffId} · {found.mobile}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">Joined {found.joinDate}</p>
              </div>
              <div className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-green-100 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="#16A34A" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {alreadyInTeam(found) ? (
            <div className="bg-amber-50 border border-amber-200 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-amber-700 text-sm font-semibold text-center">
              यह worker पहले से team में है।
            </div>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={()=>onAdd({...found,status:"active"})}
              className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2 text-base">
              <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M16 11c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3s-1.34-3-3-3M22 21v-1a4 4 0 0 0-3-3.87M1 21v-2a4 4 0 0 1 4-4h4a4 4 0 0 1 4 4v2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2"/><path d="M19 8v6M22 11h-6" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              {found.name} को Team में जोड़ें
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Not found */}
      {notFound && !found && (
        <div className="space-y-3">
          <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-4 text-center">
            <p className="text-red-600 font-bold text-sm">"{idInput}" — कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
            <p className="text-red-400 text-xs mt-1">ID या mobile number सही डालें</p>
          </div>
          <button onClick={()=>setManualMode(true)}
            className="w-full bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
            Manually जानकारी भरें →
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Manual add link */}
      {!notFound && !found && !idInput && (
        <button onClick={()=>setManualMode(true)}
          className="w-full text-blue-500 font-bold text-sm py-2 text-center active:opacity-70">
          Worker system में नहीं है? Manually जोड़ें →
        </button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

// ── Plain helper — no hooks needed ──
const sizeTotal = (row) => (parseInt(row.bundles)||0) * (parseInt(row.pcsPerBundle)||0);

// ── Stable SizeRow — outside SupervisorPanel to prevent keyboard dismiss on re-render ──
const SizeRow = React.memo(({ row, idx, onUpdate, onRemove, sizeTotal }) => {
  const total = sizeTotal(row);
  return (
    <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5">
      <select
        value={row.size}
        onChange={e => onUpdate(idx, "size", e.target.value)}
        className="w-20 shrink-0 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-1 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-red-400 text-center"
        style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
        <option value="">Size</option>
        <optgroup label="Standard">
          {["XS","S","M","L","XL","XXL","XXXL"].map(s=><option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
        </optgroup>
        <optgroup label="Waist">
          {["26","28","30","32","34","36","38","40","42"].map(s=><option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
        </optgroup>
        <optgroup label="Kids (years)">
          {["1Y","2Y","3Y","4Y","6Y","8Y","10Y","12Y","14Y"].map(s=><option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
        </optgroup>
        <optgroup label="Other">
          {["38","40","42","44","46","Free Size"].map(s=><option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>)}
        </optgroup>
      </select>
      <input
        type="number" inputMode="numeric" pattern="[0-9]*" min="1"
        value={row.bundles}
        onChange={e => onUpdate(idx, "bundles", e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Bundle"
        className="flex-1 min-w-0 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-1 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-red-400 text-center"
        style={{fontSize:"16px"}}
      />
      <input
        type="number" inputMode="numeric" pattern="[0-9]*" min="1"
        value={row.pcsPerBundle}
        onChange={e => onUpdate(idx, "pcsPerBundle", e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Pcs"
        className="flex-1 min-w-0 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-xl px-1 py-2.5 text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold focus:outline-none focus:border-red-400 text-center"
        style={{fontSize:"16px"}}
      />
      <div className="w-11 shrink-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
        {total > 0 ? (
          <>
            <p className="text-red-600 font-extrabold text-sm leading-none">{total}</p>
            <button onClick={() => onRemove(idx)} className="text-gray-300 text-xs mt-0.5 active:text-red-400">✕</button>
          </>
        ) : (
          <button onClick={() => onRemove(idx)}
            className="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center active:bg-red-100 transition">
            <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="#9CA3AF" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          </button>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
});


const SupervisorPanel = ({ onLogout }) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AppContext);
  const [tab, setTab] = useState("cutting");

  // ── State: Cutting ──
  const [cuts, setCuts] = useState([
    { id:"c1", date:"2024-01-15", style:"Men's Formal Shirt", styleId:"s1",
      sizes:[
        { size:"S",  bundles:5,  pcsPerBundle:20, total:100 },
        { size:"M",  bundles:8,  pcsPerBundle:20, total:160 },
        { size:"L",  bundles:10, pcsPerBundle:20, total:200 },
        { size:"XL", bundles:6,  pcsPerBundle:20, total:120 },
        { size:"XXL",bundles:3,  pcsPerBundle:20, total:60  },
      ],
      totalLayers:32, totalPieces:640, marker:"M-001", status:"done" },
    { id:"c2", date:"2024-01-14", style:"Kids T-Shirt", styleId:"s3",
      sizes:[
        { size:"2Y", bundles:6, pcsPerBundle:15, total:90  },
        { size:"4Y", bundles:8, pcsPerBundle:15, total:120 },
        { size:"6Y", bundles:7, pcsPerBundle:15, total:105 },
        { size:"8Y", bundles:5, pcsPerBundle:15, total:75  },
      ],
      totalLayers:26, totalPieces:390, marker:"M-002", status:"done" },
    { id:"c3", date:"2024-01-13", style:"Denim Jeans", styleId:"s4",
      sizes:[
        { size:"30", bundles:4, pcsPerBundle:10, total:40 },
        { size:"32", bundles:6, pcsPerBundle:10, total:60 },
        { size:"34", bundles:5, pcsPerBundle:10, total:50 },
      ],
      totalLayers:15, totalPieces:150, marker:"M-003", status:"pending" },
  ]);
  const [showCutForm, setShowCutForm] = useState(false);
  const EMPTY_SIZE = { size:"", bundles:"", pcsPerBundle:"" };
  const [cutForm, setCutForm]         = useState({ date:"", styleId:"", marker:"", sizes:[{ ...EMPTY_SIZE }] });
  const [cutErr,  setCutErr]          = useState("");
  const [cutSaved,setCutSaved]        = useState(false);

  // ── State: Team ──
  const [myTeam, setMyTeam]               = useState(MOCK_DB.workers.filter(w => w.status === "active"));
  const [selectedWorker, setSelectedWorker] = useState(null);
  const [showAddMember, setShowAddMember]   = useState(false);
  const [memberForm, setMemberForm]         = useState({ name:"", mobile:"", department:"", staffId:"", joinDate:"", address:"", aadhaar:"" });
  const [memberErr,  setMemberErr]          = useState("");
  const [memberSaved, setMemberSaved]       = useState(false);
  const [removeConfirm, setRemoveConfirm]   = useState(null); // worker id to confirm

  // ── State: Hourly ──
  const [reports, setReports]   = useState(MOCK_DB.hourlyReports);
  const [showHForm, setShowHForm] = useState(false);
  const TODAY = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  const [hForm, setHForm] = useState({ date:TODAY, department:"", style:"", hourSlot:"", total:"", pass:"", alter:"", reject:"" });
  const HOUR_SLOTS = ["08:00-09:00","09:00-10:00","10:00-11:00","11:00-12:00","13:00-14:00","14:00-15:00","15:00-16:00","16:00-17:00","17:00-18:00"];

  // ── State: Jobs ──
  const [jobs, setJobs]             = useState(MOCK_DB.jobs);
  const [showJobForm, setShowJobForm] = useState(false);
  const [jobForm, setJobForm]       = useState({ title:"", department:"", salary:"", experience:"", openings:"1", description:"" });
  const [applied, setApplied]       = useState({});

  // ── State: Profile ──
  const [prof, setProf]             = useState({ name:user.name, mobile:user.mobile, email:"supervisor@sharmagarments.com", department:"Stitching", language:"Hindi", address:"Ludhiana, Punjab" });
  const [editMode, setEditMode]     = useState(false);
  const [draft, setDraft]           = useState(prof);
  const [profSaved, setProfSaved]   = useState(false);

  const DEPT_COLOR = { Stitching:"#3B82F6", Finishing:"#10B981", QC:"#F59E0B", Cutting:"#EF4444", Embroidery:"#8B5CF6" };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 1: CUTTING
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════

  // Size presets — auto detect from style name keywords
  const SIZE_PRESETS = {
    standard: ["XS","S","M","L","XL","XXL","XXXL"],
    waist:    ["28","30","32","34","36","38","40","42"],
    kids:     ["2Y","4Y","6Y","8Y","10Y","12Y","14Y"],
    baby:     ["3M","6M","9M","12M","18M","24M"],
    sport:    ["XS","S","M","L","XL","XXL"],
    kurta:    ["36","38","40","42","44","46","48"],
  };

  const detectSizeSet = (styleName) => {
    const n = (styleName||"").toLowerCase();
    if (/baby|infant|newborn|3m|6m/.test(n))              return SIZE_PRESETS.baby;
    if (/kid|child|boy|girl|toddler|y|year/.test(n))  return SIZE_PRESETS.kids;
    if (/jean|denim|trouser|pant|cargo|chino|short/.test(n)) return SIZE_PRESETS.waist;
    if (/kurta|kurti|salwar|ethnic|lehenga/.test(n))       return SIZE_PRESETS.kurta;
    if (/sport|track|jersey|gym|activewear/.test(n))       return SIZE_PRESETS.sport;
    return SIZE_PRESETS.standard;
  };

  const autoFillSizes = (styleId) => {
    const style = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s=>s.id===styleId);
    if (!style) return;
    const sizeSet = detectSizeSet(style.styleName);
    setCutForm(f=>({
      ...f,
      styleId,
      sizes: sizeSet.map(size=>({ size, bundles:"", pcsPerBundle:"" }))
    }));
  };

  const CuttingTab = () => {
    const totalPcs    = cuts.reduce((s,c) => s+(+c.totalPieces||0), 0);
    const totalLayers = cuts.reduce((s,c) => s+(+c.totalLayers||0), 0);
    const done        = cuts.filter(c=>c.status==="done").length;
    const pending     = cuts.filter(c=>c.status==="pending").length;

    const grandTotal   = cutForm.sizes.reduce((s,r) => s+sizeTotal(r), 0);
    const grandBundles = cutForm.sizes.reduce((s,r) => s+(parseInt(r.bundles)||0), 0);
