    const updateSize = (idx, field, val) =>
      setCutForm(f => ({
        ...f,
        sizes: f.sizes.map((r,i) => {
          if (i === idx) return { ...r, [field]: val };
          if (idx === 0 && (field === "bundles" || field === "pcsPerBundle")) {
            return { ...r, [field]: val };
          }
          return r;
        })
      }));
    const addSizeRow = () =>
      setCutForm(f => ({ ...f, sizes: [...f.sizes, { size:"", bundles:"", pcsPerBundle:"" }] }));
    const removeSizeRow = (idx) =>
      setCutForm(f => ({ ...f, sizes: f.sizes.filter((_,i)=>i!==idx) }));

    const handleAddCut = () => {
      if (!cutForm.styleId || !cutForm.date) { setCutErr("Date और Style जरूरी हैं।"); return; }
      const validSizes = cutForm.sizes.filter(r => r.size && r.bundles && r.pcsPerBundle);
      if (validSizes.length === 0) { setCutErr("कम से कम एक size की पूरी जानकारी भरें।"); return; }
      const style = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === cutForm.styleId);
      const sizesWithTotal = validSizes.map(r => ({ ...r, bundles:+r.bundles, pcsPerBundle:+r.pcsPerBundle, total:sizeTotal(r) }));
      const totalP = sizesWithTotal.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.total, 0);
      const totalL = sizesWithTotal.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.bundles||0), 0);
      const isEdit = !!cutForm._editId;
      if (isEdit) {
        setCuts(prev => prev.map(c => c.id===cutForm._editId ? {
          ...c, date:cutForm.date, styleId:cutForm.styleId,
          style:style?.styleName||"", marker:cutForm.marker,
          sizes:sizesWithTotal, totalPieces:totalP, totalLayers:totalL
        } : c));
      } else {
        setCuts(prev => [{
          id:"c"+Date.now(), date:cutForm.date, styleId:cutForm.styleId,
          style:style?.styleName||"", marker:cutForm.marker,
          sizes:sizesWithTotal, totalPieces:totalP, totalLayers:totalL, status:"done"
        }, ...prev]);
      }
      setCutForm({ date:"", styleId:"", marker:"", sizes:[{ size:"", bundles:"", pcsPerBundle:"" }] });
      setCutErr(""); setShowCutForm(false); setCutSaved(true);
      setTimeout(()=>setCutSaved(false), 2500);
    };


    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {/* Hero */}
        <div className="rounded-3xl overflow-hidden" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#7F1D1D 0%,#DC2626 50%,#F97316 100%)"}}>
          <div className="p-6">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
              <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-xl bg-white/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><circle cx="6" cy="18" r="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M20 4L8.12 15.88M14.47 14.48L20 20M8.12 8.12L12 12" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-red-100 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Cutting Department</p>
            </div>
            <p className="text-white text-5xl font-black">{totalPcs.toLocaleString()}</p>
            <p className="text-red-200 text-sm mt-1">Total Pieces · {totalLayers} bundles</p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mt-5">
              {[
                { label:"Done",    val:done,    color:"text-green-300" },
                { label:"Pending", val:pending, color:"text-amber-300" },
                { label:"Styles",  val:new Set(cuts.map(c=>c.styleId)).size, color:"text-white" },
              ].map(x=>(
                <div key={x.label} className="bg-white/15 rounded-2xl py-3 text-center backdrop-blur-sm">
                  <p className={"text-2xl font-black "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
                  <p className="text-red-200 text-xs mt-0.5">{x.label}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="h-1 bg-white/20">
            <div className="h-1 bg-white/60 transition-all" style={{width:cuts.length?(done/cuts.length*100)+"%":"0%"}}/>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Add Button */}
        <button onClick={()=>{setShowCutForm(true);setCutErr("");setCutForm({date:TODAY,styleId:"",marker:"",sizes:[{size:"",bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}]});}}
          className="w-full bg-red-500 active:bg-red-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-red-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          नई Cutting Entry डालें
        </button>

        {cutSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Cutting entry add हो गई!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Cutting Records</p>

        <div className="space-y-3">
          {cuts.map(c=>(
            <div key={c.id} className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className={`h-1.5 ${c.status==="done"?"bg-green-500":"bg-amber-400"}`}/>
              <div className="p-4">
                {/* Card header */}
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-3">
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold truncate">{c.style}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{c.date}{c.marker?" · "+c.marker:""}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
                    <button onClick={()=>{
                      setShowCutForm(true); setCutErr("");
                      setCutForm({ _editId:c.id, date:c.date, styleId:c.styleId, marker:c.marker||"",
                        sizes: c.sizes.map(r=>({size:r.size,bundles:String(r.bundles),pcsPerBundle:String(r.pcsPerBundle)})) });
                    }} className="w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 flex items-center justify-center active:bg-orange-100 transition">
                      <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                    </button>
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full ${c.status==="done"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border border-green-200":"bg-amber-50 text-amber-600 border border-amber-200"}`}>
                      {c.status==="done"?"✓ Done":"⏳"}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>

                {/* Summary row */}
                <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mb-3">
                  {[
                    { label:"Total Pieces", value:c.totalPieces?.toLocaleString()||"0", color:"text-red-600",    bg:"bg-red-50"    },
                    { label:"Bundles",      value:c.totalLayers||c.sizes?.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.bundles||0),0)||0, color:"text-orange-600", bg:"bg-orange-50" },
                    { label:"Sizes",        value:c.sizes?.length||"—",                color:"text-gray-700",  bg:"bg-gray-50"   },
                  ].map(s=>(
                    <div key={s.label} className={`${s.bg} rounded-xl p-2.5 text-center`}>
                      <p className={"font-extrabold text-base "+s.color}>{s.value}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{s.label}</p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>

                {/* Size breakdown */}
                {c.sizes && c.sizes.length > 0 && (
                  <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-gray-100">
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-4 px-3 py-1.5 bg-gray-100">
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold">Size</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold text-center">Bundles</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold text-center">Pcs/Bundle</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold text-right">Total</p>
                    </div>
                    {c.sizes.map((row,i)=>(
                      <div key={i} className={`grid grid-cols-4 px-3 py-2 ${i%2===0?"bg-white":"bg-gray-50/60"} border-t border-gray-100`}>
                        <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{row.size}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm text-center">{row.bundles}</p>
                        <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm text-center">{row.pcsPerBundle}</p>
                        <p className="text-red-600 font-extrabold text-sm text-right">{row.total}</p>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-4 px-3 py-2 bg-red-50 border-t border-red-100">
                      <p className="text-red-700 font-extrabold text-sm col-span-3">TOTAL</p>
                      <p className="text-red-700 font-extrabold text-sm text-right">{c.totalPieces}</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Add Cutting Modal */}
        <Modal open={showCutForm} onClose={()=>setShowCutForm(false)} title={cutForm._editId?"Cutting Edit करें":"नई Cutting Entry"}>
          <div className="space-y-5">
            {cutErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{cutErr}</div>}

            {/* Date + Style */}
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <Input label="Date" type="date" value={cutForm.date} max={TODAY}
                onChange={e=>setCutForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Marker No." value={cutForm.marker} placeholder="M-001"
                onChange={e=>setCutForm(f=>({...f,marker:e.target.value}))}/>
            </div>
            <Select label="Style / Order" value={cutForm.styleId}
              onChange={e=>{ if(!cutForm._editId) autoFillSizes(e.target.value); else setCutForm(f=>({...f,styleId:e.target.value})); }}>
              <option value="">-- Style चुनें --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.map(s=><option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
            </Select>

            {/* Size rows */}
            <div>
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                <p className="text-gray-700 text-sm font-extrabold">Size-wise Layers</p>
                <span className="text-red-500 text-xs font-bold bg-red-50 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-red-100">
                  {grandTotal > 0 ? `Total: ${grandTotal} pcs` : "0 pcs"}
                </span>
              </div>

              {/* Header */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-1.5 px-1">
                <p className="w-20 shrink-0 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Size</p>
                <p className="flex-1 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Bundles</p>
                <p className="flex-1 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Pcs/Bundle</p>
                <p className="w-11 shrink-0 text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold text-center">Total</p>
              </div>
              {/* First row hint */}
              {cutForm.sizes.length > 1 && (!cutForm.sizes[0].bundles || !cutForm.sizes[0].pcsPerBundle) && (
                <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-orange-50 border border-orange-200 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 mb-1">
                  <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M12 8v4M12 16h.01" stroke="#F97316" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                  <p className="text-orange-600 text-xs font-semibold">पहली row में Bundles & Pcs/Bundle डालें — सभी sizes में auto-fill होगा</p>
                </div>
              )}

              <div className="space-y-2">
                {cutForm.sizes.map((row,idx)=>(
                  <SizeRow
                    key={idx}
                    row={row}
                    idx={idx}
                    onUpdate={updateSize}
                    onRemove={removeSizeRow}
                    sizeTotal={sizeTotal}
                  />
                ))}
              </div>

              {/* Total row */}
              {grandTotal > 0 && (
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-red-50 border border-red-100 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mt-3">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-red-700 text-xs font-bold">{grandBundles} total bundles</p>
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-xs">{cutForm.sizes.filter(r=>r.size).length} sizes</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-red-700 font-black text-2xl">{grandTotal}</p>
                    <p className="text-red-400 text-xs">total pieces</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}

              {/* Quick preset buttons */}
              <div className="mt-2 space-y-2">
                <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Quick Fill</p>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1.5">
                  {[
                    { label:"Standard", sizes:["XS","S","M","L","XL","XXL","XXXL"] },
                    { label:"Waist",    sizes:["28","30","32","34","36","38","40"] },
                    { label:"Kids",     sizes:["2Y","4Y","6Y","8Y","10Y","12Y"] },
                    { label:"Baby",     sizes:["3M","6M","9M","12M","18M","24M"] },
                    { label:"Kurta",    sizes:["36","38","40","42","44","46"] },
                  ].map(preset=>(
                    <button key={preset.label}
                      onClick={()=>setCutForm(f=>({...f, sizes:preset.sizes.map(s=>({size:s,bundles:"",pcsPerBundle:""}))}))}
                      className="bg-gray-100 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl active:bg-red-50 active:border-red-300 active:text-red-600 transition">
                      {preset.label}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Add custom size row */}
              <button onClick={addSizeRow}
                className="mt-1 w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5 bg-gray-50 border border-dashed border-gray-300 text-gray-500 font-bold text-sm py-2.5 rounded-xl active:bg-gray-100 transition">
                <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                Custom Size जोड़ें
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowCutForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-red-500 hover:bg-red-600" onClick={handleAddCut}>{cutForm._editId?"Save Changes →":"Add Cutting →"}</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 2: MY TEAM (TAILORS)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const TeamTab = () => {
    const byDept = myTeam.reduce((acc,w)=>{ (acc[w.department]||(acc[w.department]=[])).push(w); return acc; },{});
    const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
    const filtered = search ? myTeam.filter(w=>w.name.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())||w.staffId.toLowerCase().includes(search.toLowerCase())) : null;

    if (selectedWorker) {
      const w = myTeam.find(x=>x.id===selectedWorker);
      const wEntries = MOCK_DB.workEntries.filter(e=>e.workerId===selectedWorker);
      const totalAmt = wEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.amount, 0);
      const totalPcs = wEntries.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.pieces, 0);
      const color    = DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B";
      return (
        <div className="px-4 pt-4 pb-28 space-y-4">
          <button onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(null)}
            className="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-blue-500 font-bold text-sm active:opacity-70 transition">
            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M19 12H5M5 12l7 7M5 12l7-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
            My Team पर वापस
          </button>
          {/* Worker Hero */}
          <div className="rounded-3xl p-6 text-center" style={{background:`linear-gradient(135deg,${color}dd,#0F172A)`}}>
            <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-white/20 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white text-3xl font-black mx-auto mb-3 backdrop-blur-sm border border-white/20">
              {w.name.charAt(0)}
            </div>
            <h3 className="text-white text-xl font-extrabold">{w.name}</h3>
            <p className="text-white/60 text-sm mt-0.5">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
            <p className="text-white/40 text-xs">Joined {w.joinDate}</p>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mt-5">
              {[
                { label:"Pieces",   val:totalPcs,         color:"text-white"       },
                { label:"Earnings", val:"Rs "+totalAmt,   color:"text-green-300"   },
                { label:"Entries",  val:wEntries.length,  color:"text-white"       },
              ].map(x=>(
                <div key={x.label} className="bg-white/15 rounded-2xl py-3 text-center">
                  <p className={"font-extrabold text-sm "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
                  <p className="text-white/50 text-xs">{x.label}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Work Entries */}
          <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Work Entries</p>
          {wEntries.length===0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई work entry नहीं</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className="space-y-2">
              {wEntries.map(e=>(
                <div key={e.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3.5 flex items-center gap-3 shadow-sm">
                  <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0" style={{background:color+"22"}}>
                    <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 12l2 2 4-4" stroke={color} strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke={color} strokeWidth="1.5"/></svg>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{e.styleName}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.operation} · {e.date}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                    <p className="text-green-600 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {e.amount}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      );
    }

    const listToShow = filtered || [];

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {/* Hero */}
        <div className="rounded-3xl p-6" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1E3A8A,#3B82F6 60%,#06B6D4)"}}>
          <p className="text-blue-100 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">My Team</p>
          <p className="text-white text-5xl font-black">{myTeam.length}</p>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Active Tailors · {Object.keys(byDept).length} departments</p>
          <div className="flex gap-2 mt-4 flex-wrap">
            {Object.entries(byDept).map(([dept,workers])=>(
              <span key={dept} className="bg-white/20 backdrop-blur-sm rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-white text-xs font-bold border border-white/20">
                {dept}: {workers.length}
              </span>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Add Member Button */}
        <button onClick={()=>{setShowAddMember(true);setMemberErr("");setMemberForm({name:"",mobile:"",department:"",staffId:"SG0"+(myTeam.length+2),joinDate:TODAY,address:"",aadhaar:""});}}
          className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M16 11c1.66 0 3-1.34 3-3s-1.34-3-3-3M22 21v-1a4 4 0 0 0-3-3.87M1 21v-2a4 4 0 0 1 4-4h4a4 4 0 0 1 4 4v2" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="3" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2"/><path d="M19 8v6M22 11h-6" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          नया Member जोड़ें
        </button>

        {memberSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">नया member team में add हो गया!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Search */}
        <div className="relative">
          <svg className="absolute left-3.5 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-gray-400" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="11" cy="11" r="7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M16.5 16.5L21 21" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          <input value={search} onChange={e=>setSearch(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Worker नाम या ID से ढूंढें..."
            className="w-full bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-2xl pl-10 pr-4 py-3 text-sm text-gray-900 placeholder-gray-400 focus:outline-none focus:border-blue-400 shadow-sm" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
        </div>

        {/* Worker list or search results */}
        {search ? (
          <div className="space-y-2">
            {listToShow.length===0 ? (
              <div className="text-center py-10 bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
                <p className="text-gray-400">कोई worker नहीं मिला</p>
              </div>
            ) : listToShow.map(w=>(
              <WorkerCard key={w.id} w={w} onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(w.id)}/>
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : (
          Object.entries(byDept).map(([dept,workers])=>(
            <div key={dept} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50"
                style={{borderLeftWidth:"4px",borderLeftColor:DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B",borderLeftStyle:"solid"}}>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">{dept}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{workers.length} active tailors</p>
                </div>
                <span className="text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full"
                  style={{background:(DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B")+"22",color:DEPT_COLOR[dept]||"#64748B"}}>
                  {workers.length}
                </span>
              </div>
              <div className="divide-y divide-gray-50">
                {workers.map(w=><WorkerCard key={w.id} w={w} onClick={()=>setSelectedWorker(w.id)}/>)}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))
        )}

        {/* Add Member Modal — ID Lookup */}
        <Modal open={showAddMember} onClose={()=>{setShowAddMember(false);setMemberErr("");setMemberForm({name:"",mobile:"",department:"",staffId:"",joinDate:"",address:"",aadhaar:""});}} title="Worker ID से जोड़ें">
          <AddMemberById
            myTeam={myTeam}
            onAdd={(worker)=>{
              setMyTeam(prev=>[...prev,{...worker,status:"active"}]);
              setShowAddMember(false);
              setMemberSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setMemberSaved(false),3000);
            }}
            onClose={()=>setShowAddMember(false)}
            TODAY={TODAY}
          />
        </Modal>

        {/* Remove Confirm Modal */}
        {removeConfirm && (() => {
          const w = myTeam.find(x=>x.id===removeConfirm);
          if (!w) return null;
          return (
            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-end justify-center" style={{background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.5)"}}>
              <div className="bg-white w-full max-w-lg rounded-t-3xl p-6 space-y-4 shadow-2xl">
                <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-red-100 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center mx-auto">
                  <svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
                    <path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4h8v2M19 6l-1 14H6L5 6" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                  </svg>
                </div>
                <div className="text-center">
                  <h3 className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-lg">{w.name} को हटाएं?</h3>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-sm mt-1">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
                  <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-2">इस worker को आपकी team से remove किया जाएगा।</p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-3">
                  <button onClick={()=>setRemoveConfirm(null)}
                    className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                    Cancel
                  </button>
                  <button onClick={()=>{
                    setMyTeam(prev=>prev.filter(x=>x.id!==removeConfirm));
                    if (selectedWorker===removeConfirm) setSelectedWorker(null);
                    setRemoveConfirm(null);
                  }}
                    className="flex-1 bg-red-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3.5 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-red-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">
                    हाँ, हटाएं
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })()}

      </div>
    );
  };

  const WorkerCard = ({w, onClick}) => (
    <div className="flex items-center group">
      <button onClick={onClick}
        className="flex-1 flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3.5 active:bg-gray-50 transition text-left min-w-0">
        <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center font-extrabold text-white text-sm shrink-0"
          style={{background:DEPT_COLOR[w.department]||"#64748B"}}>
          {w.name.charAt(0)}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
          <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">{w.name}</p>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{w.staffId} · {w.department}</p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-1.5 shrink-0 mr-2">
          <div className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-green-500"/>
          <span className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Active</span>
          <span className="text-gray-300 text-lg ml-1">›</span>
        </div>
      </button>
      {/* Remove button */}
      <button onClick={e=>{e.stopPropagation();setRemoveConfirm(w.id);}}
        className="shrink-0 mr-3 w-8 h-8 rounded-xl bg-red-50 border border-red-200 flex items-center justify-center active:bg-red-100 transition">
        <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none">
          <path d="M17 7l-10 10M7 7l10 10" stroke="#EF4444" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/>
        </svg>
      </button>
    </div>
  );

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 3: HOURLY REPORT
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const HourlyTab = () => {
    const totalPass   = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.pass||0),0);
    const totalAlter  = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.alter||0),0);
    const totalReject = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.reject||0),0);
    const totalPcs    = reports.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.total||0),0);
    const avgPass     = totalPcs ? (totalPass/totalPcs*100).toFixed(1) : 0;

    const addReport = () => {
      const total = +hForm.total, pass = +hForm.pass;
      if (!hForm.department || !hForm.hourSlot || !hForm.total) return;
      setReports(prev=>[...prev,{ ...hForm, id:"h"+Date.now(), passPercent:total?(pass/total*100).toFixed(1):0 }]);
      setHForm({ date:TODAY, department:"", style:"", hourSlot:"", total:"", pass:"", alter:"", reject:"" });
      setShowHForm(false);
    };

    const bySlot = reports.reduce((acc,h)=>{ (acc[h.hourSlot]||(acc[h.hourSlot]=[])).push(h); return acc; },{});

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {/* Hero */}
        <div className="rounded-3xl overflow-hidden" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#0F172A 0%,#1E293B 50%,#B45309 100%)"}}>
          <div className="p-6">
            <p className="text-amber-300 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Quality Overview</p>
            <div className="flex items-end gap-3">
              <p className="text-white text-5xl font-black">{avgPass}%</p>
              <p className="text-slate-400 text-sm mb-2">pass rate</p>
            </div>
            <div className="w-full h-2 bg-white/10 rounded-full mt-3 overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-2 rounded-full transition-all" style={{width:avgPass+"%", background:"linear-gradient(90deg,#F59E0B,#10B981)"}}/>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mt-4">
              {[
                { label:"Total",  val:totalPcs,    color:"text-white"       },
                { label:"Pass",   val:totalPass,   color:"text-green-400"   },
                { label:"Alter",  val:totalAlter,  color:"text-amber-400"   },
                { label:"Reject", val:totalReject, color:"text-red-400"     },
              ].map(x=>(
                <div key={x.label} className="bg-white/10 rounded-2xl py-2.5 text-center">
                  <p className={"font-extrabold text-lg "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
                  <p className="text-slate-500 text-xs">{x.label}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <button onClick={()=>setShowHForm(true)}
          className="w-full bg-amber-500 active:bg-amber-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-amber-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Add Hourly Report
        </button>

        <p className="text-xs font-extrabold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider">Hour-wise Data</p>

        <div className="space-y-3">
          {Object.entries(bySlot).sort().map(([slot,rows])=>{
            const sp   = rows.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.pass||0),0);
            const st   = rows.reduce((s,r)=>s+(+r.total||0),0);
            const pct  = st?(sp/st*100).toFixed(1):0;
            const good = +pct>=90;
            return (
              <div key={slot} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
                {/* Slot header */}
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3" style={{background:"#1E293B"}}>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="w-6 h-6 rounded-lg bg-white/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                      <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8"/><path d="M12 8v4l2.5 2.5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-white font-extrabold text-sm">{slot}</span>
                  </div>
                  <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full ${good?"bg-green-500 text-white":"bg-red-500 text-white"}`}>
                    {pct}% Pass
                  </span>
                </div>
                {/* Pass bar */}
                <div className="h-1 bg-gray-100">
                  <div className="h-1 transition-all" style={{width:pct+"%", background:good?"#10B981":"#EF4444"}}/>
                </div>
                {/* Dept rows */}
                {rows.map((r,i)=>(
                  <div key={r.id} className={`grid grid-cols-5 px-4 py-3 text-sm items-center gap-2 ${i>0?"border-t border-gray-50":""}`}>
                    <div className="col-span-2">
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-semibold text-xs">{r.department}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs truncate">{r.style}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-gray-700 font-bold text-xs">{r.total}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Total</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-green-600 font-bold text-xs">{r.pass}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Pass</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-center">
                      <p className="text-red-500 font-bold text-xs">{r.reject}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">Rej</p>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        <Modal open={showHForm} onClose={()=>setShowHForm(false)} title="Add Hourly Report">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <Input label="Date" type="date" value={hForm.date} max={TODAY} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Select label="Department" value={hForm.department} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,department:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Department --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=><option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <Select label="Style" value={hForm.style} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,style:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Style --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.map(s=><option key={s.id} value={s.styleName}>{s.styleName}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <Select label="Hour Slot" value={hForm.hourSlot} onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,hourSlot:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Time Slot चुनें --</option>
              {HOUR_SLOTS.map(s=><option key={s}>{s}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <Input label="Total" type="number" value={hForm.total} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,total:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Pass" type="number" value={hForm.pass} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,pass:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Alter" type="number" value={hForm.alter} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,alter:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Reject" type="number" value={hForm.reject} placeholder="0" onChange={e=>setHForm(f=>({...f,reject:e.target.value}))}/>
            </div>
            {hForm.total && hForm.pass && (
              <div className="rounded-xl p-3 text-center" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#F59E0B22,#10B98122)"}}>
                <p className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-xl">{((+hForm.pass/+hForm.total)*100).toFixed(1)}% Pass Rate</p>
              </div>
            )}
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowHForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-amber-500 hover:bg-amber-600" onClick={addReport}>Submit Report →</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 4: JOBS
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const JobsTab = () => {
    const active = jobs.filter(j=>j.status==="active");
    const postJob = () => {
      if (!jobForm.title||!jobForm.department) return;
      setJobs(prev=>[{ id:"j"+Date.now(), ...jobForm, openings:+jobForm.openings||1, status:"active", applications:0, postedDate:TODAY }, ...prev]);
      setJobForm({ title:"", department:"", salary:"", experience:"", openings:"1", description:"" });
      setShowJobForm(false);
    };
    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        <div className="rounded-3xl p-6" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1D4ED8,#3B82F6 60%,#06B6D4)"}}>
          <p className="text-blue-100 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">Job Openings</p>
          <p className="text-white text-5xl font-black">{active.length}</p>
          <p className="text-blue-200 text-sm mt-1">Active positions · Sharma Garments</p>
          <p className="text-blue-300 text-xs mt-3">{jobs.reduce((s,j)=>s+(j.applications||0),0)} total applications received</p>
        </div>

        <button onClick={()=>setShowJobForm(true)}
          className="w-full bg-blue-500 active:bg-blue-600 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-blue-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Post New Job
        </button>

        <div className="space-y-3">
          {jobs.map(job=>(
            <div key={job.id} className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
              <div className="h-1 bg-gradient-to-r from-blue-400 to-cyan-400"/>
              <div className="p-4">
                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-2 mb-3">
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{job.title}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{job.department}{job.postedDate?" · "+job.postedDate:""}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex flex-col items-end gap-1 shrink-0">
                    <span className={`text-xs font-bold px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border ${job.status==="active"?"bg-green-50 text-green-600 border-green-200":"bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 border-gray-200"}`}>
                      {job.status==="active"?"Active":"Closed"}
                    </span>
                    <span className="text-xs text-gray-400">{job.openings} posts</span>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                  {job.salary && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.salary}</span>}
                  {job.experience && <span className="bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 text-gray-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.experience}</span>}
                  {job.applications > 0 && <span className="bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 text-blue-600 text-xs font-semibold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl">{job.applications} applied</span>}
                </div>
                {job.description && <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs leading-relaxed">{job.description}</p>}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        <Modal open={showJobForm} onClose={()=>setShowJobForm(false)} title="Post New Job">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            <Input label="Job Title" value={jobForm.title} placeholder="जैसे Senior Tailor, Cutter..." onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,title:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Select label="Department" value={jobForm.department} onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,department:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Department --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=><option key={d.id} value={d.name}>{d.name}</option>)}
            </Select>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
              <Input label="Salary Range" value={jobForm.salary} placeholder="Rs 8,000-12,000" onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,salary:e.target.value}))}/>
              <Input label="Openings" type="number" min="1" value={jobForm.openings} onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,openings:e.target.value}))}/>
            </div>
            <Input label="Experience Required" value={jobForm.experience} placeholder="जैसे 2+ years" onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,experience:e.target.value}))}/>
            <Input label="Description" value={jobForm.description} placeholder="Job details..." onChange={e=>setJobForm(f=>({...f,description:e.target.value}))}/>
            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowJobForm(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1" onClick={postJob}>Post Job →</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // TAB 5: PROFILE
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const ProfileTab = () => {
    const saveProf = () => { setProf(draft); setEditMode(false); setProfSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setProfSaved(false),2500); };
    const fld = (label, key, type="text", opts=null) => (
      <div key={key} className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
        <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs font-semibold mb-1">{label}</p>
        {editMode ? (
          opts ? (
            <select value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}>
              {opts.map(o=><option key={o}>{o}</option>)}
            </select>
          ) : (
            <input type={type} value={draft[key]} onChange={e=>setDraft(p=>({...p,[key]:e.target.value}))}
              className="w-full bg-gray-50 border border-orange-300 rounded-xl px-3 py-2 text-gray-900 text-sm font-semibold focus:outline-none" style={{fontSize:"16px"}}/>
          )
        ) : (
          <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{prof[key]||"—"}</p>
        )}
      </div>
    );

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">
        {profSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Profile save हो गई!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Avatar hero */}
        <div className="rounded-3xl p-6 text-center" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#1E3A8A,#1E293B)"}}>
          <div className="w-20 h-20 bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-400 to-cyan-500 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center text-white text-3xl font-black mx-auto mb-3 shadow-lg shadow-blue-500/30">
            {prof.name.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}
          </div>
          <h2 className="text-white text-xl font-extrabold">{prof.name}</h2>
          <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm mt-0.5">{prof.mobile}</p>
          <div className="mt-3 inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-blue-500/20 border border-blue-400/30 rounded-full px-4 py-1.5">
            <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-blue-400"/>
            <span className="text-blue-300 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-wider">Supervisor · {prof.department}</span>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Stats row */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3">
          {[
            { label:"Team",    val:myTeam.length,   color:"text-blue-600",  bg:"bg-blue-50"  },
            { label:"Reports", val:reports.length,  color:"text-amber-600", bg:"bg-amber-50" },
            { label:"Cuts",    val:cuts.length,     color:"text-red-600",   bg:"bg-red-50"   },
          ].map(x=>(
            <div key={x.label} className={`${x.bg} rounded-2xl py-4 text-center`}>
              <p className={"text-2xl font-black "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
              <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{x.label}</p>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Edit / Save */}
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          {editMode ? (
            <>
              <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(false);setDraft(prof);}}
                className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">Cancel</button>
              <button onClick={saveProf}
                className="flex-1 bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-orange-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition">Save Changes</button>
            </>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={()=>{setEditMode(true);setDraft(prof);}}
              className="flex-1 flex items-center justify-center gap-2 bg-white border-2 border-orange-400 text-orange-500 font-bold text-sm py-3 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.12 2.12 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4z" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              Edit Profile
            </button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Personal Info */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100 flex items-center justify-between">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Personal Info</p>
            {editMode && <span className="text-orange-400 text-xs font-bold">Editing...</span>}
          </div>
          {fld("Full Name",   "name")}
          {fld("Mobile",      "mobile",     "tel")}
          {fld("Email",       "email",      "email")}
          {fld("Department",  "department", "text", MOCK_DB.departments.map(d=>d.name))}
          {fld("Address",     "address")}
          {fld("Language",    "language",   "text", ["Hindi","English","Hindi + English"])}
        </div>

        {/* Factory Info */}
        <div className="bg-white border border-gray-100 rounded-2xl shadow-sm overflow-hidden">
          <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-gray-50 border-b border-gray-100">
            <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs font-extrabold uppercase tracking-wider">Factory Info</p>
          </div>
          {[
            { label:"Factory",       value:user.tenantName||"Sharma Garments" },
            { label:"Team Size",     value:myTeam.length+" tailors"           },
            { label:"Reports Today", value:reports.length+" entries"          },
            { label:"Status",        value:"Active Supervisor"                 },
          ].map(item=>(
            <div key={item.label} className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3.5 border-b border-gray-50 last:border-0">
              <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">{item.label}</span>
              <span className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-bold">{item.value}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        <button onClick={onLogout}
          className="w-full bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 font-bold text-sm py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition">
          Sign Out / लॉगआउट
        </button>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  // WORK ENTRIES TAB (Approve / Reject)
  // ══════════════════════════════════════════
  const WorkEntriesTab = () => {
    const [wEntries, setWEntries] = useState(() =>
      MOCK_DB.workEntries.map(e => ({ ...e, status: e.status || "pending" }))
    );
    const [filter,   setFilter]   = useState("pending");
    const [selected, setSelected] = useState(null);
    const [showAdd,  setShowAdd]  = useState(false);
    const [addErr,   setAddErr]   = useState("");
    const [addSaved, setAddSaved] = useState(false);
    const EMPTY_ADD = { workerId:"", date:TODAY, styleId:"", operationId:"", pieces:"", note:"" };
    const [addForm,  setAddForm]  = useState(EMPTY_ADD);

    const filtered = filter === "all" ? wEntries : wEntries.filter(e => e.status === filter);

    const updateStatus = (id, status) => {
      setWEntries(prev => prev.map(e => e.id === id ? { ...e, status } : e));
      setSelected(null);
    };

    const pendingCount = wEntries.filter(e => e.status === "pending").length;

    const selWorker   = MOCK_DB.workers.find(w => w.id === addForm.workerId);
    const selStyle    = MOCK_DB.styles.find(s => s.id === addForm.styleId);
    const selOp       = MOCK_DB.operations.find(o => o.id === addForm.operationId);
    const addAmount   = selOp ? (parseFloat(selOp.pieceRate) * (parseInt(addForm.pieces)||0)) : 0;

    const handleAddEntry = () => {
      if (!addForm.workerId)   { setAddErr("Worker चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.date)       { setAddErr("Date डालें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.styleId)    { setAddErr("Style चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.operationId){ setAddErr("Operation चुनें।"); return; }
      if (!addForm.pieces || +addForm.pieces < 1) { setAddErr("Pieces डालें।"); return; }
      const w = MOCK_DB.workers.find(x => x.id === addForm.workerId);
      const s = MOCK_DB.styles.find(x => x.id === addForm.styleId);
      const o = MOCK_DB.operations.find(x => x.id === addForm.operationId);
      setWEntries(prev => [{
        id: "we"+Date.now(),
        workerId:  w.id,        workerName: w.name,
        staffId:   w.staffId,   department: w.department,
        styleId:   s.id,        styleName:  s.styleName,
        operationId: o.id,      operation:  o.name,
        date:      addForm.date,
        pieces:    +addForm.pieces,
        pieceRate: o.pieceRate,
        amount:    addAmount,
        note:      addForm.note,
        status:    "approved",
      }, ...prev]);
      setShowAdd(false); setAddErr(""); setAddForm(EMPTY_ADD);
      setAddSaved(true); setTimeout(()=>setAddSaved(false), 2500);
    };

    const statusMeta = {
      pending:  { label:"Pending",  bar:"bg-amber-400",  text:"text-amber-600",  bg:"bg-amber-50",  border:"border-amber-200"  },
      approved: { label:"Approved", bar:"bg-green-500",  text:"text-green-600",  bg:"bg-green-50",  border:"border-green-200"  },
      rejected: { label:"Rejected", bar:"bg-red-400",    text:"text-red-500",    bg:"bg-red-50",    border:"border-red-200"    },
    };

    const selEntry = selected ? wEntries.find(e => e.id === selected) : null;

    return (
      <div className="px-4 pt-5 pb-28 space-y-4">

        {/* Hero */}
        <div className="rounded-3xl overflow-hidden" style={{background:"linear-gradient(135deg,#064E3B 0%,#059669 60%,#34D399 100%)"}}>
          <div className="p-6">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
              <div className="w-7 h-7 rounded-xl bg-white/20 flex items-center justify-center">
                <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 11l3 3L22 4" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
              </div>
              <p className="text-green-100 text-xs font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Work Entries</p>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-end justify-between">
              <div>
                <p className="text-white text-5xl font-black">{pendingCount}</p>
                <p className="text-green-200 text-sm mt-1">Pending approval</p>
              </div>
              <div className="text-right">
                <p className="text-green-200 text-xs">Total entries</p>
                <p className="text-white text-2xl font-black">{wEntries.length}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 mt-5">
              {[
                { label:"Pending",  val:wEntries.filter(e=>e.status==="pending").length,  color:"text-amber-300"  },
                { label:"Approved", val:wEntries.filter(e=>e.status==="approved").length, color:"text-white"      },
                { label:"Rejected", val:wEntries.filter(e=>e.status==="rejected").length, color:"text-red-300"    },
              ].map(x=>(
                <div key={x.label} className="bg-white/15 rounded-2xl py-3 text-center backdrop-blur-sm">
                  <p className={"text-2xl font-black "+x.color}>{x.val}</p>
                  <p className="text-green-200 text-xs mt-0.5">{x.label}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="h-1 bg-white/20">
            <div className="h-1 bg-white/70 transition-all"
              style={{width: wEntries.length ? (wEntries.filter(e=>e.status==="approved").length / wEntries.length * 100)+"%" : "0%"}}/>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Add Entry button */}
        <button onClick={()=>{setShowAdd(true);setAddErr("");setAddForm(EMPTY_ADD);}}
          className="w-full bg-green-600 active:bg-green-700 text-white font-extrabold text-base py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-green-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
          <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
          Work Entry Add करें
        </button>

        {addSaved && (
          <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-200 rounded-2xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center gap-2">
            <div className="w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-green-500 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 12 12" fill="none"><path d="M2 6l3 3 5-5" stroke="white" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
            </div>
            <p className="text-green-700 text-sm font-semibold">Entry add हो गई — Approved!</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Filter tabs */}
        <div className="flex bg-gray-100 rounded-2xl p-1 gap-0.5">
          {["pending","approved","rejected","all"].map(f=>(
            <button key={f} onClick={()=>setFilter(f)}
              className={"flex-1 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold transition relative "+(filter===f?"bg-white text-gray-900 shadow-sm":"text-gray-400")}>
              {f==="all"?"All":f.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+f.slice(1)}
              {f==="pending" && pendingCount > 0 && (
                <span className="absolute -top-1 -right-1 w-4 h-4 bg-amber-400 text-white text-[9px] font-black rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  {pendingCount}
                </span>
              )}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Entry list */}
        <div className="space-y-2">
          {filtered.length === 0 && (
            <div className="text-center py-12 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100">
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">कोई entry नहीं</p>
            </div>
          )}
          {filtered.map(e => {
            const m = statusMeta[e.status] || statusMeta.pending;
            return (
              <button key={e.id} onClick={()=>setSelected(e.id)}
                className="w-full bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-100 shadow-sm overflow-hidden text-left active:scale-[0.99] transition">
                <div className={"h-1.5 "+m.bar}/>
                <div className="px-4 py-3.5 flex items-start gap-3">
                  {/* Worker avatar */}
                  <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-green-100 flex items-center justify-center text-green-700 font-extrabold text-sm shrink-0">
                    {(e.workerName||"W").charAt(0)}
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm truncate">{e.workerName}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs">{e.styleName} · {e.operation}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs mt-0.5">{e.date} · {e.staffId}</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="text-right shrink-0">
                    <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm">Rs {(+e.amount||0).toFixed(0)}</p>
                    <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{e.pieces} pcs</p>
                    <span className={"text-xs font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full mt-1 inline-block "+m.bg+" "+m.text}>
                      {m.label}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Detail / Action bottom sheet */}
        {/* Add Entry Modal */}
        <Modal open={showAdd} onClose={()=>setShowAdd(false)} title="नई Work Entry जोड़ें">
          <div className="space-y-4">
            {addErr && <div className="bg-red-50 border border-red-200 rounded-xl p-3 text-red-600 text-sm">{addErr}</div>}

            {/* Worker select */}
            <Select label="Worker" value={addForm.workerId}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,workerId:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Worker चुनें --</option>
              {myTeam.filter(w=>w.status==="active").map(w=>(
                <option key={w.id} value={w.id}>{w.name} ({w.staffId})</option>
              ))}
            </Select>

            <Input label="Date" type="date" value={addForm.date} max={TODAY}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,date:e.target.value}))}/>

            <Select label="Style / Order" value={addForm.styleId}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,styleId:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Style चुनें --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.styles.filter(s=>s.status==="active").map(s=>(
                <option key={s.id} value={s.id}>{s.styleName}</option>
              ))}
            </Select>

            <Select label="Operation" value={addForm.operationId}
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,operationId:e.target.value}))}>
              <option value="">-- Operation चुनें --</option>
              {MOCK_DB.operations.map(o=>(
                <option key={o.id} value={o.id}>{o.name} — Rs {o.pieceRate}/pc</option>
              ))}
            </Select>

            <Input label="Pieces" type="number" min="1" value={addForm.pieces} placeholder="कितने pieces?"
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,pieces:e.target.value}))}/>

            {addAmount > 0 && (
              <div className="bg-green-50 border border-green-100 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 flex items-center justify-between">
                <div>
                  <p className="text-green-700 font-extrabold text-xl">Rs {addAmount.toFixed(2)}</p>
                  <p className="text-green-400 text-xs">{addForm.pieces} pcs × Rs {selOp?.pieceRate}/pc</p>
                </div>
                {selWorker && (
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-green-700 font-bold text-sm">{selWorker.name}</p>
                    <p className="text-green-400 text-xs">{selWorker.staffId}</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            <Input label="Note (optional)" value={addForm.note} placeholder="कोई comment?"
              onChange={e=>setAddForm(f=>({...f,note:e.target.value}))}/>

            <div className="flex gap-3">
              <Btn variant="secondary" className="flex-1" onClick={()=>setShowAdd(false)}>Cancel</Btn>
              <Btn className="flex-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-700" onClick={handleAddEntry}>Add Entry →</Btn>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Modal>

        {selEntry && (() => {
          const m = statusMeta[selEntry.status] || statusMeta.pending;
          return (
            <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-end" style={{background:"rgba(0,0,0,0.5)"}}>
              <div className="bg-white w-full max-w-lg mx-auto rounded-t-3xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden">
                {/* Handle */}
                <div className="flex justify-center pt-3 pb-1">
                  <div className="w-10 h-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full"/>
                </div>
                {/* Header */}
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-5 py-3 border-b border-gray-100">
                  <h3 className="font-extrabold text-gray-900">Entry Detail</h3>
                  <button onClick={()=>setSelected(null)}
                    className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-gray-100 flex items-center justify-center text-gray-500 font-bold active:bg-gray-200">✕</button>
                </div>
                {/* Content */}
                <div className="px-5 py-4 space-y-4">
                  {/* Worker info */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-green-100 flex items-center justify-center text-green-700 font-extrabold text-lg">
                      {(selEntry.workerName||"W").charAt(0)}
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold">{selEntry.workerName}</p>
                      <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{selEntry.staffId} · {selEntry.department}</p>
                    </div>
                    <span className={"ml-auto text-xs font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full "+m.bg+" "+m.text+" border "+m.border}>
                      {m.label}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  {/* Entry details */}
                  <div className="bg-gray-50 rounded-2xl p-4 space-y-2">
                    {[
                      { label:"Style",      value:selEntry.styleName   },
                      { label:"Operation",  value:selEntry.operation   },
                      { label:"Date",       value:selEntry.date        },
                      { label:"Pieces",     value:selEntry.pieces+" pcs" },
                      { label:"Piece Rate", value:"Rs "+selEntry.pieceRate+"/pc" },
                      { label:"Amount",     value:"Rs "+(+selEntry.amount||0).toFixed(2), bold:true },
                    ].map(row=>(
                      <div key={row.label} className="flex items-center justify-between">
                        <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">{row.label}</p>
                        <p className={"text-sm "+(row.bold?"text-green-600 font-extrabold":"text-gray-900 font-bold")}>{row.value}</p>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                  {/* Actions */}
                  {selEntry.status === "pending" ? (
                    <div className="flex gap-3 pb-2">
                      <button onClick={()=>updateStatus(selEntry.id,"rejected")}
                        className="flex-1 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                        <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2.2" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg>
                        Reject
                      </button>
                      <button onClick={()=>updateStatus(selEntry.id,"approved")}
                        className="flex-1 bg-green-500 text-white font-extrabold py-4 rounded-2xl shadow-md shadow-green-200 active:scale-[0.98] transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
                        <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M5 13l4 4L19 7" stroke="white" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/></svg>
                        Approve
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="flex gap-3 pb-2">
                      <button onClick={()=>updateStatus(selEntry.id,"pending")}
                        className="flex-1 bg-gray-100 text-gray-600 font-bold py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition text-sm">
                        Pending पर वापस
                      </button>
                      {selEntry.status === "approved" ? (
                        <button onClick={()=>updateStatus(selEntry.id,"rejected")}
                          className="flex-1 bg-red-50 border border-red-200 text-red-500 font-bold py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition text-sm">
                          Reject करें
                        </button>
                      ) : (
                        <button onClick={()=>updateStatus(selEntry.id,"approved")}
                          className="flex-1 bg-green-500 text-white font-bold py-3.5 rounded-2xl active:scale-[0.98] transition text-sm">
                          Approve करें
                        </button>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          );
        })()}
      </div>
    );
  };


  // ── TAB CONFIG ──
  const TABS = [
    { id:"cutting", label:"Cutting",
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="6" cy="6" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/><circle cx="6" cy="18" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7"/><path d="M20 4L8.12 15.88M14.47 14.48L20 20M8.12 8.12L12 12" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"team",    label:"My Team",
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M3 21v-2a4 4 0 0 1 4-4h4a4 4 0 0 1 4 4v2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/><circle cx="17" cy="7" r="2" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M21 21v-1a3 3 0 0 0-2-2.83" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg> },
    { id:"entries", label:"Entries",
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><path d="M9 11l3 3L22 4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/><path d="M21 12v7a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H5a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h11" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"hourly",  label:"Hourly",
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M12 7v5l3 3" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round"/></svg> },
    { id:"profile", label:"Profile",
      icon:<svg width="22" height="22" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"><circle cx="12" cy="8" r="4" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" fill="none"/><path d="M4 20c0-4 3.6-7 8-7s8 3 8 7" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" fill="none"/></svg> },
  ];

  const TAB_COLORS = { cutting:"text-red-500", team:"text-blue-500", entries:"text-green-600", hourly:"text-amber-500", jobs:"text-indigo-500", profile:"text-purple-500" };
  const TAB_DOT    = { cutting:"bg-red-500",   team:"bg-blue-500",   entries:"bg-green-500",   hourly:"bg-amber-500",   jobs:"bg-indigo-500",   profile:"bg-purple-500"  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50" style={{fontFamily:"'DM Sans','Segoe UI',sans-serif"}}>
      {/* Header */}
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-20 bg-white border-b border-gray-100 shadow-sm">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 max-w-lg mx-auto">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2.5">
            <GarmentLogo size={34}/>
            <div>
              <p className="text-gray-900 font-extrabold text-sm leading-tight">
                {tab==="cutting"?"Cutting":tab==="team"?"My Team":tab==="entries"?"Work Entries":tab==="hourly"?"Hourly Report":tab==="jobs"?"Jobs":"Profile"}
              </p>
              <p className="text-gray-400 text-xs">{user.name} · Supervisor</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-blue-500 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-extrabold text-sm shadow-sm shadow-blue-200">
            {user.name.charAt(0)}
          </div>
        </div>
      </header>

      <main className="max-w-lg mx-auto">
        {tab==="cutting" && <CuttingTab/>}
        {tab==="team"    && <TeamTab/>}
        {tab==="entries" && <WorkEntriesTab/>}
        {tab==="hourly"  && <HourlyTab/>}
        {tab==="profile" && <ProfileTab/>}
      </main>

      {/* Bottom Nav — stays below keyboard using env(safe-area-inset-bottom) */}
      <nav className="fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 z-30 bg-white border-t border-gray-100 shadow-[0_-4px_20px_rgba(0,0,0,0.06)]" style={{paddingBottom:"env(safe-area-inset-bottom)"}}>
        <div className="flex max-w-lg mx-auto">
          {TABS.map(t=>(
            <button key={t.id} onClick={()=>{ setTab(t.id); setSelectedWorker(null); }}
              className={"flex-1 flex flex-col items-center py-3 gap-0.5 transition "+(tab===t.id?TAB_COLORS[t.id]:"text-gray-400")}>
              <div className={tab===t.id?"scale-110 transition-transform":""}>{t.icon}</div>
              <span className="text-xs font-bold">{t.label}</span>
              {tab===t.id && <div className={"w-4 h-0.5 rounded-full mt-0.5 "+TAB_DOT[t.id]}/>}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      </nav>
    </div>
  );
};

const NAV_ITEMS = [
  { id: "dashboard",    icon: "home",       label: "Home",          roles: ["admin", "supervisor", "worker", "contractor"] },
  { id: "staff-payment",icon: "payment",    label: "Staff Payment", roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "self-entry",   icon: "self-entry", label: "My Work",       roles: ["worker"] },
  { id: "workers",      icon: "workers",    label: "Workers",       roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "styles",       icon: "styles", label: "Styles",         roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "operations",   icon: "operations", label: "Operations",     roles: ["admin"] },
  { id: "departments",  icon: "departments", label: "Departments",    roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "hourly",       icon: "hourly", label: "Hourly",         roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "jobs",         icon: "jobs", label: "Jobs",           roles: ["admin", "supervisor", "worker", "contractor"] },
  { id: "export",       icon: "export", label: "Export",         roles: ["admin", "supervisor"] },
  { id: "profile",      icon: "profile", label: "Profile",        roles: ["admin", "supervisor", "worker", "contractor"] },
];

const BOTTOM_NAV = ["dashboard", "self-entry", "jobs", "profile"];

// ============================================================
// MAIN APP
// ============================================================
export default function App() {
  const [user, setUser] = useState(null);
  const [page, setPage] = useState("dashboard");

  // Fix: keyboard pushing up bottom nav on mobile
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const meta = document.querySelector("meta[name=viewport]");
    if (meta) meta.content = "width=device-width, initial-scale=1, viewport-fit=cover, interactive-widget=resizes-visual";
  }, []);
  const [pageHistory, setPageHistory] = useState([]);
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(false);

  const handleLogin = (u) => { setUser(u); setPage("dashboard"); setPageHistory([]); };
  const handleLogout = () => { setUser(null); setPage("dashboard"); setPageHistory([]); };

  const navigate = (p) => {
    if (p !== page) {
      setPageHistory(prev => [...prev, page]);
    }
    setPage(p);
    setSidebarOpen(false);
  };

  const goBack = () => {
    if (pageHistory.length > 0) {
      const prev = pageHistory[pageHistory.length - 1];
      setPageHistory(h => h.slice(0, -1));
      setPage(prev);
    } else {
      setPage("dashboard");
    }
    setSidebarOpen(false);
  };

  if (!user) return <LoginPage onLogin={handleLogin} />;

  // Worker के लिए अलग dedicated panel
  if (user.role === "worker") {
    return (
      <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate: () => {} }}>
        <WorkerPanel onLogout={handleLogout} />
      </AppContext.Provider>
    );
  }

  // Supervisor के लिए अलग dedicated panel
  if (user.role === "supervisor") {
    return (
      <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate: () => {} }}>
        <SupervisorPanel onLogout={handleLogout} />
      </AppContext.Provider>
    );
  }


  const bottomNav = allowedNav.filter(n => BOTTOM_NAV.includes(n.id));

  const renderPage = () => {
    switch (page) {
      case "dashboard": return <Dashboard />;
      case "staff-payment": return <StaffPaymentFull />;
      case "work-entry": return <WorkEntry />;

      case "self-entry": return <SelfEntry />;
      case "workers": return <Workers />;
      case "styles": return <Styles />;
      case "operations": return <Operations />;
      case "departments": return <Departments />;
      case "payments": return <Payments />;
      case "hourly": return <HourlyReports />;
      case "jobs": return <JobPortal />;

      case "export":  return <ExportCenter />;
      case "profile": return <Profile onLogout={handleLogout} />;
      default: return <Dashboard />;
    }
  };

  return (
    <AppContext.Provider value={{ user, navigate }}>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-white text-gray-900 font-sans"
        style={{ fontFamily: "'DM Sans', 'Segoe UI', sans-serif" }}>

        {/* Desktop Sidebar */}
        <aside className={`fixed top-0 left-0 h-full w-64 bg-gray-50 border-r border-gray-200 z-40 flex flex-col
          transform transition-transform duration-300 lg:translate-x-0 ${sidebarOpen ? "translate-x-0" : "-translate-x-full"}`}>
          
          {/* Logo */}
          <div className="p-5 border-b border-gray-200">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <GarmentLogo size={40} />
              <div>
                <p className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm leading-tight">Garment Factory</p>
                <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs">Management SaaS</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* User info */}
          <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-200">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-orange-500 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm">
                {user.name.charAt(0)}
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0">
                <p className="text-gray-900 text-sm font-medium truncate">{user.name}</p>
                <p className="text-gray-700 text-xs capitalize">{user.role}</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Nav */}
          <nav className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto py-3 px-2">
            {allowedNav.map(item => (
              <button key={item.id} onClick={() => navigate(item.id)}
                className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl mb-0.5 text-sm font-semibold transition-all
                  ${page === item.id ? "bg-orange-500 text-white shadow-md shadow-orange-500/20" : "text-gray-900 hover:bg-gray-200 hover:text-gray-900"}`}>
                <NavIcon id={item.id} size={17} />
                {item.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </nav>

          <div className="p-4 border-t border-gray-200">
            <button onClick={handleLogout} className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-red-400 hover:bg-red-500/10 text-sm font-medium transition">
              <svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
              <path d="M6 14H3a1 1 0 0 1-1-1V3a1 1 0 0 1 1-1h3M10 11l3-3-3-3M13 8H6" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
            </svg> Sign Out
            </button>
          </div>
        </aside>

        {/* Sidebar overlay (mobile) */}
        {sidebarOpen && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-30 lg:hidden" onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)} />
        )}

        {/* Main content */}
        <div className="lg:pl-64 flex flex-col min-h-screen">
          {/* Top bar */}
          <header className="sticky top-0 z-20 bg-white/95 backdrop-blur border-b border-gray-200 px-4 py-3 shadow-sm">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">

                {/* Mobile hamburger */}
                <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)} className="lg:hidden p-2 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-xl transition">
                  <div className="space-y-1.5">
                    <div className="w-5 h-0.5 bg-gray-800 rounded" />
                    <div className="w-4 h-0.5 bg-gray-600 rounded" />
                    <div className="w-5 h-0.5 bg-gray-800 rounded" />
                  </div>
                </button>

                {/* Back button — show on any non-dashboard page */}
                {page !== "dashboard" && (
                  <button
                    onClick={goBack}
                    className="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl bg-orange-50 hover:bg-orange-100 text-orange-600 text-sm font-bold transition border border-orange-200 active:scale-95">
                    ← Back
                  </button>
                )}

                <div>
                  <h2 className="text-gray-900 font-bold text-sm flex items-center gap-1.5">
                    <NavIcon id={page} size={15} className="text-orange-500 shrink-0" />
                    {NAV_ITEMS.find(n => n.id === page)?.label || "Dashboard"}
                  </h2>
                  <p className="text-gray-500 text-xs hidden sm:block">{user.tenantName}</p>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                <button className="relative p-2 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-xl transition">
                  <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                    <path d="M10 2a6 6 0 0 0-6 6v3l-1.5 2.5h15L16 11V8a6 6 0 0 0-6-6z" stroke="#374151" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinejoin="round"/>
                    <path d="M8.5 16.5a1.5 1.5 0 0 0 3 0" stroke="#374151" strokeWidth="1.5" strokeLinecap="round"/>
                  </svg>
                  <span className="absolute top-1 right-1 w-2 h-2 bg-orange-500 rounded-full" />
                </button>
                <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-orange-500 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold text-sm">
                  {user.name.charAt(0)}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </header>

          {/* Page content */}
          <main className="flex-1 p-4 pb-24 lg:pb-6 max-w-5xl mx-auto w-full">
            {renderPage()}
          </main>
        </div>

        {/* Mobile Bottom Nav */}
        <nav className="lg:hidden fixed bottom-0 left-0 right-0 bg-gray-50/95 backdrop-blur border-t border-gray-200 z-20 px-2 py-2 safe-area-pb">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-around">
            {bottomNav.map(item => (
              <button key={item.id} onClick={() => navigate(item.id)}
                className={`flex flex-col items-center gap-0.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-xl transition-all
                  ${page === item.id ? "text-orange-400" : "text-gray-700 hover:text-gray-900"}`}>
                <NavIcon id={item.id} size={22} className={`transition-transform ${page === item.id ? "scale-110" : ""}`} />
                <span className="text-xs font-medium">{item.label}</span>
                {page === item.id && <div className="w-1 h-1 bg-orange-500 rounded-full mt-0.5" />}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </nav>
      </div>
    </AppContext.Provider>
  );
}
